bibhrad astīti vyapadiśyate antarbhāvāc ca tenāsau karmaṇā na sakarmakaḥ  BVaky prāk ca sattābhisaṃbandhān mukhyā sattā kathaṃ bhavet asaṃś ca nāsteḥ kartā syād upacāras tu pūrvavat  BVaky tasmād bhinneṣu dharmeṣu virodhiṣv avirodhinīm virodhikhyāpanāyaiva śabdais tais tair upāśritām  BVaky abhinnakālām artheṣu bhinnakāleṣv avasthitām pravṛttihetuṃ sarveṣāṃ śabdānām aupacārikīm  BVaky etāṃ sattāṃ padārtho hi na kaś cid ativartate sā ca saṃpratisattāyāḥ pṛthag bhāśye nidarśitā  BVaky pradeśasyaikadeśaṃ vā parato vā nirūpaṇam viparyayam abhāvaṃ vā vyavahāro nuvartate  BVaky yathendriyasya vaiguṇyān mātrādhyāropavān iva jāyate pratyayo rthebhyas tathaivoddeśajā matiḥ  BVaky akṛtsnaviṣayābhāsaṃ śabdaḥ pratyayam āśritaḥ artham āhānyarūpeṇa svarūpeṇānirūpitam  BVaky rūpaṇavyapadeśābhyāṃ laukike vartmani sthitau jñānaṃ praty abhilāpaṃ ca sadṛśau bālapaṇḍitau  BVaky sarvārtharūpatā śuddhir jñānasya nirupāśrayā tato py asya parāṃ śuddhim eke prāhur arūpikām  BVaky upaplavo hi jñānasya bāhyākārānupātitā kāluṣyam iva tat tasya saṃsarge vyatibhedajam  BVaky yathā ca jñānam ālekhād aśuddhau vyavatiṣṭhate tathopāśrayavān arthaḥ svarūpād viprakṛṣyate  BVaky evam arthasya śabdasya jñānasya ca viparyaye bhāvābhāvāv abhedena vyavahārānupātinau  BVaky yathā bhāvam upāśritya tadabhāvo nugamyate tathābhāvam upāśritya tadbhāvo py anugamyate  BVaky nābhāvo jāyate bhāvo naiti bhāvo nupākhyatām ekasmād ātmano nanyau bhāvābhāvau vikalpitau  BVaky abhāvasyānupākhyatvāt kāraṇaṃ na prasādhakam sopākhyasya tu bhāvasya kāraṇaṃ kiṃ kariśyati  BVaky tasmāt sarvam abhāvo vā bhāvo vā sarvam iṣyate na tv avasthāntaraṃ kiṃ cid ekasmāt satyataḥ sthitam  BVaky tasmān nābhāvam icchanti ye loke bhāvavādinaḥ abhāvavādino vāpi na bhāvaṃ tattvalakṣaṇam  BVaky advaye caiva sarvasmin svabhāvād ekalakṣaṇe parikalpeṣu maryādā vicitraivopalabhyate  BVaky catasro hi yathāvasthā nirupākhye prakalpitāḥ evaṃ dvaividhyam apy etad bhāvābhāvavyapāśrayam  BVaky avirodhī virodhī vā sann asan vāpi yuktitaḥ kramavān akramo vāpi nābhāva upapadyate  BVaky avirodhī virodhī vā sann asan vāpi tattvataḥ kramavān akramo vāpi tena bhāvo na vidyate  BVaky abhāve triṣu kāleṣu na bhedasyāsti saṃbhavaḥ tasminn asati bhāve pi traikālyaṃ nāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky ātmatattvaparityāgaḥ parato nopapadyate ātmatattvaṃ tu parataḥ svato vā nopakalpate  BVaky tattve virodho nānātva upakāro na kaś cana tattvānyatvaparityāge vyavahāro nivartate  BVaky yatra draṣṭā ca dṛśyaṃ ca darśanaṃ cāvikalpitam tasyaivārthasya satyatvaṃ śritās trayyantavedinaḥ  BVaky sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣaṃ vā yasmād āhur viśeṣavat śabdās tasmād asatyeṣu bhedeṣv eva vyavasthitāḥ  BVaky na hy abhāvasya sadbhāve bhāvasyātmā prahīyate na cābhāvasya nāstitve bhāvasyātmā prasūyate  BVaky na śābaleyasyāstitvaṃ bāhuleyasya bādhakam na śābaleyo nāstīti bāhuleyaḥ prakalpate  BVaky abhāvo yadi vastu syāt tatreyaṃ syāt vicāraṇā tataś ca tadabhāve pi syād vicāryam idaṃ punaḥ  BVaky avastu syād atītaṃ yad vyavahārasya gocaram tatra vastugato bhedo na nirvacanam arhati  BVaky apade rthe padanyāsaḥ kāraṇasya na vidyate atha ca prāgasadbhāvaḥ kāraṇe sati dṛṣyate  BVaky kā tasya prāgavastheti vastvāśritam idaṃ punaḥ prāg avastheti na hy etad dvayam apy asty avastuni  BVaky na cordhvam asti nāstīti vacanāyānibandhanam alaṃ syād apadasthānam etad vācaḥ pracakṣate  BVaky atyadbhutā tv iyaṃ vṛttir yad abhāgaṃ yad akramam bhāvānāṃ prāg abhūtānām ātmatattvaṃ prakāśate  BVaky vikalpotthāpitenaiva sarvo bhāvena laukikaḥ mukhyeneva padārthena vyavahāro vidhīyate  BVaky bhāvaśaktim ataś caināṃ manyante nityavādinaḥ bhāvam eva kramam prāhur na bhāvād aparaḥ kramaḥ  BVaky kramān na yaugapadyasya kaś cid bhedo sti tattvataḥ yathaiva bhāvān nābhāvaḥ kaś cid anyo vasīyate  BVaky kālasyāpy aparaṃ kālaṃ nirdiśanty eva laukikāḥ na ca nirdeśamātreṇa vyatireko nugamyate  BVaky ādhāraṃ kalpayan buddhyā nābhāve vyavatiṣṭhate avastuṣv api notprekṣā kasya cit pratibadhyate  BVaky tasmāc chaktivibhāgena nityaḥ sadasadātmakaḥ eko rthaḥ śabdavācyatve bahurūpaḥ prakāśate  BVaky vyavahāraś ca lokasya padārthaiḥ parikalpitaiḥ śāstre padārthaḥ kāryārthaṃ laukikaḥ pravibhajyate  BVaky  Bhūyodravyasamuddeśaḥsaṃsargarūpāt saṃbhūtāḥ saṃvidrūpād apoddhṛtāḥ śāstre vibhaktā vākyārthāt prakṛtipratyayārthavat  BVaky nimittabhūtāḥ sādhutve śāstrād anumitātmakāḥ ke cit padārthā vakṣyante saṃkśepeṇa yathāgamam  BVaky vastūpalakṣaṇaṃ yatra sarvanāma prayujyate dravyam ity ucyate so rto bhedyatvena vivakśitaḥ  BVaky  Guṇasamudeśasaṃsargi bhedakaṃ yad yat savyāpāraṃ pratīyate guṇatvaṃ paratantratvāt tasya śāstra udāhṛtam  BVaky dravyasyāvyapadeśasya ya upādīyate guṇaḥ bhedako vyapadeśāya tatprakarṣo bhidhīyate  BVaky sarvasyaiva pradhānasya na vinā bhedahetunā prakarṣo vidyate nāpi śabdasyopaiti vācyatām  BVaky vidyamānāḥ pradhāneṣu na sarve bhedahetavaḥ viśeṣaśabdair ucyante vyāvṛttārthābhidhāyibhiḥ  BVaky vastūpalakṣaṇe tatra viśeṣo vyāpṛto yadi prakarṣo niyamābhāvāt syād avijñātahetukaḥ  BVaky sarvaṃ ca sarvato vaśyaṃ niyamena prakṛṣyate saṃsargiṇā nimittena nikṛṣṭenādhikena vā  BVaky nāpekṣate nimittaṃ ca prakarṣe vyāpṛtaṃ yadi dravyasya syād upādānaṃ prakarṣaṃ praty anarthakaṃ  BVaky savyāpāro guṇas tasmāt svaprakarṣanibandhanaḥ dravyātmānaṃ bhinatty eva svaprakarṣaṃ niveśayan  BVaky arūpaṃ pararūpeṇa dravyam ākhyāyate yathā aprakarṣaṃ prakarṣeṇa guṇasyāviśyate tathā  BVaky  Diksamuddeśadik sādhanam kriyā kāla iti vastvabhidhāyinaḥ śaktirūpe padārthānām atyantam anavasthitāḥ  BVaky vyatirekasya yo hetur avadhipratipādyayoḥ ṛjv ity evam yato nyena vinā buddhiḥ pravartate  BVaky karmano jātibhedānām abhivyaktir yadāśrayā sā svair upādhibhir bhinnā śaktir dig iti kathyate  BVaky parāparatve mūrtināṃ deśabhedanibandhane tata eva prakalpete kramarūpe tu kālataḥ  BVaky ākāśasya pradeśena bhāgaiś cānyaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak sā saṃyogavibhāgānām upādhitvāya kalpate  BVaky diśo vyavasthā deśānāṃ digvyavasthā na vidyate śaktayaḥ khalu bhāvānām upakāraprabhāvitāḥ  BVaky pratyastarūpā bhāveṣu dik pūrvety abhidhīyate pūrvabuddhir yato dik sā samākhyāmātram anyathā  BVaky svāṅgād vyavasthā yā loke na tasyām niyatā diśaḥ pratyaṅmukhasya yat paścāt tat purastād viparyaye  BVaky deśavyavasthāniyamo dikṣu na vyavatiṣṭhate rūḍham apy aparatvena pūrvam ity abhidhīyate  BVaky ato bhāṣitapuṃskatvāt puṃvadbhāvo na sidhyati asminn arthe na śabdena prasavaḥ kva cid ucyate  BVaky dikśakter abhidhāne tu niyataṃ diśi darśanam pūrvādināṃ yathā ṣaṣṭer jīvitasyāvadhāraṇe  BVaky chāyābhābhyāṃ nagādīnām bhāgabhedaḥ prakalpate ataddharmasu bhāveṣu bhāgabhedo na kalpate  BVaky paramāṇor abhāgasya diśā bhāgo vidhīyate bhāgaprakalpanāśaktiṃ prathamāṃ tāṃ pracakṣate  BVaky adeśāś cāpy abhāgāś ca niṣkramā nirupāśrayāḥ bhāvāḥ saṃsargirūpāt tu śaktibhedaḥ prakalpate  BVaky nirbhāgātmakatā tulyā paramāṇor ghaṭasya ca bhāgaḥ śaktyantaraṃ tatra parimāṇaṃ ca yat tayoḥ  BVaky yataḥ prakalpate bhedo bhedas tatrāpi dṛśyate adṛṣṭoparatiṃ bhedam ato yuktataraṃ viduḥ  BVaky sarvatra tasya kāryasya darśanād vibhur iṣyate vibhutvam etad evāhur anyaḥ kāyavatāṃ vidhiḥ  BVaky caitanyavat sthitā loke dikkālaparikalpanā prakṛtiṃ prāṇināṃ tāṃ hi ko nyathā sthāpayiṣyati  BVaky saṃkaro vyavahārāṇāṃ prakṛteḥ syād viparyaye tasmāt tyajann imān bhāvān punar evāvalambate  BVaky tasyās tu śakteḥ pūrvādi bhedo bhāvāntarāśrayaḥ bhinnā dik tena bhedena bhedāyaivopakalpate  BVaky avadhitvena cāpekṣā yoge diglakṣaṇo vidhiḥ pūrvam asyeti ṣaṣṭhy eva dṛṣṭā dharmāntarāśraye  BVaky pūrvādināṃ viparyāso dṛṣṭaś cāvadhyasaṃkare ṛjv etad asyety etac ca liṅgaṃ na vyatikīryate  BVaky antaḥkaraṇadharmo vā bahir evaṃ prakāśate asyāṃ tv antarbahirbhāvaḥ prakriyāyāṃ na vidyate  BVaky ekatvam āsāṃ śaktīnāṃ nānātvaṃ veti kalpane avastupatite jñātvā satyato na parāmṛśet  BVaky vikalpātītatattveṣu saṃketopanibandhanāḥ bhāveṣu vyavahārā ye lokas tatrānugamyate  BVaky naikatvam asty anānātvaṃ vinaikatvena netarat paramārthe tayor eṣa bhedo tyantaṃ na vidyate  BVaky na śaktīnāṃ tathā bhedo yathā śaktimatām sthitiḥ na ca laukikam ekatvaṃ tāsām ātmasu vidyate  BVaky naikatvaṃ vyavatiṣṭheta nānātvaṃ cen na kalpayet nānātvaṃ cāvahīyeta yady ekatvaṃ na kalpayet  BVaky  Sādhanasamuddeśasvāśraye samavetānāṃ tadvad evāśrayāntare kriyāṇām abhiniṣpattau sāmarthyaṃ sādhanaṃ viduḥ  BVaky śaktimātrāsamūhasya viśvasyānekadharmaṇaḥ sarvadā sarvathā bhāvāt kva cit kiṃ cid vivakṣyate  BVaky sādhanavyavahāraś ca buddhyavasthānibandhanaḥ sann asan vārtharūpeṣu bhedo buddhyā prakalpyate  BVaky buddhyā samīhitaikatvān pañcālān kurubhir yadā punar vibhajate vaktā tadāpāyaḥ pratīyate  BVaky śabdopahitarūpāṃś ca buddher viṣayatāṃ gatān pratyakṣam iva kaṃsādīn sādhanatvena manyate  BVaky buddhipravṛttirūpaṃ ca samāropyābhidhātṛbhiḥ artheṣu śaktibhedānāṃ kriyate parikalpanā  BVaky vyaktau padārthe śabdāder janyamānasya karmaṇaḥ sādhanatvaṃ tathā siddhaṃ buddhirūpaprakalpitam  BVaky svatantraparatantratve kramarūpaṃ ca darśitam nirīheṣv api bhāveṣu kalpanopanibandhanam  BVaky śaktayaḥ śaktimantaś ca sarve saṃsargavādinām bhāvās teṣv asvaśabdeṣu sādhanatvaṃ nirūpyate  BVaky ghaṭasya dṛśikarmatve mahattvādīni sādhanam rūpasya dṛśikarmatve rūpatvādīni sādhanam  BVaky svaiḥ sāmānyaviśeṣaiś ca śaktimanto rasādayaḥ niyatagrahaṇā loke śaktayas tās tathāśrayaiḥ  BVaky indriyārthamanaḥkartṛ saṃbandhaḥ sādhanaṃ kva cit yad yadā yadanugrāhi tat tadā tatra sādhanam  BVaky svaśabdair abhidhāne tu sa dharmo nābhidhīyate vibhaktyādibhir evāsāv upakāraḥ pratīyate  BVaky nimittabhāvo bhāvānām upakārārtham āśritaḥ natir āvarjanety evaṃ siddhaḥ sādhanam iṣyate  BVaky sa tebhyo vyatirikto vā teṣām ātmaiva vā tathā vyatirekam upāśritya sādhanatvena kalpyate  BVaky saṃdarśanaṃ prārthanāyāṃ vyavasāye tv anantarā vyavasāyas tathārambhe sādhanatvāya kalpate  BVaky pūrvasmin yā kriyā saiva parasmin sādhanaṃ matā saṃdarśane tu caitanyaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ viduḥ  BVaky niṣpattimātre kartṛtvaṃ sarvatraivāsti kārake vyāpārabhedāpekṣāyāṃ karaṇatvādisaṃbhavaḥ  BVaky putrasya janmani yathā pitroḥ kartṛtvam ucyate ayam asyām iyaṃ tv asmād iti bhedo vivakṣayā  BVaky guṇakriyāṇāṃ kartāraḥ kartrā nyakkṛtaśaktayaḥ nyaktāyām api saṃpūrṇaiḥ svair vyāpāraiḥ samanvitāḥ  BVaky karaṇatvādibhir jñātāḥ kriyābhedānupātibhiḥ svātantryam uttaraṃ labdhvā pradhāne yānti kartṛtām  BVaky yathā rājñā niyukteṣu yoddhṛtvaṃ yoddhṛṣu sthitam teṣu vṛttau tu labhate rājā jayaparājayau  BVaky tathā kartrā niyukteṣu sarveṣv ekārthakāriṣu kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvāder uttaraṃ na virudhyate  BVaky anāśrite tu vyāpāre nimittaṃ hetur iṣyate āśritāvadhibhāvaṃ tu lakṣaṇe lakṣaṇaṃ viduḥ  BVaky dravyādiviṣayo hetuḥ kārakaṃ niyatakriyam kartā kartrantarāpekṣaḥ kriyāyāṃ hetur iṣyate  BVaky kriyāyai karaṇaṃ tasya dṛṣṭaḥ pratinidhis tathā hetvarthā tu kriyā tasmān na sa pratinidhīyate  BVaky prātilomyānulomyābhyāṃ hetur arthasya sādhakaḥ tādarthyam ānulomyena hetutvānugataṃ tu tat  BVaky sarvatra sahajā śaktir yāvaddravyam avasthitā kriyākāle tv abhivyakter āśrayād upakāriṇī  BVaky kuḍyasyāvaraṇe śaktir asyādīnāṃ vidāraṇe sarvadā sa tu san dharmaḥ kriyākāle nirūpyate  BVaky svāngasaṃyoginaḥ pāśā daityānāṃ vāruṇā yathā vyajyante vijigīṣūṇāṃ dravyāṇāṃ śaktayas tathā  BVaky taikṣṇyagauravakāṭhinya saṃsthānaiḥ svair asir yadā chedyaṃ prati vyāpriyate śaktimān gṛhyate tadā  BVaky prān nimittāntarodbhūtaṃ kriyāyāḥ kaiś cid iṣyate sādhanaṃ sahajaṃ kaiś cit kriyānyaiḥ pūrvam iṣyate  BVaky pravṛttir eva prathamaṃ kva cid apy anapāśritā śaktīr ekādhikaraṇe srotovad apakarṣati  BVaky apūrvaṃ kālaśaktiṃ vā kriyāṃ vā kālam eva vā tam evamlaksanam bhāvam ke cid āhuh katham ca na  BVaky nityāḥ ṣaṭ śaktayo anyeṣāṃ bhedābhedasamanvitāḥ kriyāsaṃsiddhaye rtheṣu jātivat samavasthitāḥ  BVaky dravyākārādibhedena tāś cāparimitā iva dṛśyante tattvam āsāṃ tu ṣaṭ śaktīr nātivartate  BVaky nimittabhedād ekaiva bhinnā śaktiḥ pratīyate ṣoḍhā kartṛtvam evāhus tatpravṛtter nibandhanam  BVaky tattve vā vyatireke vā vyatiriktaṃ tad ucyate śabdapramāṇako lokaḥ sa śāstreṇānugamyate  BVaky paramārthe tu naikatvaṃ pṛthaktvād bhinnalakṣaṇam pṛthaktvaikatvarūpeṇa tattvam eva prakāśate  BVaky yat pṛthaktvam asaṃdigdhaṃ tad ekatvān na bhidyate yad ekatvam asaṃdigdhaṃ tat pṛthaktvān na bhidyate  BVaky dyauḥ kṣamā vāyur ādityaḥ sāgarāḥ sarito diśaḥ antaḥkaraṇatattvasya bhāgā bahir avasthitāḥ  BVaky kālavicchedarūpeṇa tad evaikam avasthitam sa hy apūrvāparo bhāvaḥ kramarūpeṇa lakṣyate  BVaky dṛṣṭo hy avyatireke pi vyatireko nvaye sati vṛkṣādyarthānvayas tasmād vibhaktyartho nya iṣyate  BVaky sāmānyaṃ kārakaṃ tasya saptādyā bhedayonayaḥ ṣaṭ karmākhyādibhedena śeṣabhedas tu saptamī  BVaky atha karmādhikāraḥnirvartyaṃ ca vikāryaṃ ca prāpyaṃ ceti tridhā matam tatrepsitatamaṃ karma caturdhānyat tu kalpitam  BVaky audāsīnyena yat prāpyaṃ yac ca kartur anīpsitam saṃjñāntarair anākhyātaṃ yad yac cāpy anyapūrvakam  BVaky satī vāvidyamānā vā prakṛtiḥ pariṇāminī yasya nāśriyate tasya nirvartyatvaṃ pracakṣate  BVaky prakṛtes tu vivakṣāyāṃ vikāryaṃ kaiś cid anyathā nirvartyaṃ ca vikāryaṃ ca karma śāstre pradarśitam  BVaky yad asaj jāyate sad vā janmanā yat prakāśyate tan nirvartyaṃ vikāryaṃ ca karma dvedhā vyavasthitam  BVaky prakṛtyucchedasaṃbhūtaṃ kiṃ cit kāṣṭhādibhasmavat kiṃ cid guṇāntarotpattyā suvarṇādivikāravat  BVaky kriyākṛtā viśeṣāṇāṃ siddhir yatra na gamyate darśanād anumānād vā tat prāpyam iti kathyate  BVaky viśeṣalābhaḥ sarvatra vidyate darśanādibhiḥ keṣāṃ cit tadabhivyakti siddhir dṛṣṭiviṣādiṣu  BVaky ābhāsopagamo vyaktiḥ soḍhatvam iti karmaṇaḥ viśeṣāḥ prāpyamāṇasya kriyāsiddhau vyavasthitāḥ  BVaky nirvartyādiṣu tat pūrvam anubhūya svatantratām kartrantarāṇāṃ vyāpāre karma saṃpadyate tataḥ  BVaky tadvyāpāraviveke pi svavyāpāre vyavasthitam karmāpadiṣṭāṃllabhate kva cic chāstrāśrayān vidhīn  BVaky nivṛttapreṣaṇaṃ karma svakriyāvayave sthitam nivartamāne karmatve sve kartṛtve vatiṣṭhate  BVaky tāni dhātvantarāṇy eva pacisidhyativad viduḥ bhede pi tulyarūpatvād ekatvaparikalpanā  BVaky ekadeśe samūhe ca vyāpārāṇāṃ pacādayaḥ svabhāvataḥ pravartante tulyarūpasamanvitāḥ  BVaky nyagbhāvanā nyagbhavanaṃ ruhau śuddhe pratīyate nyagbhāvanā nyagbhavanaṃ ṇyante pi pratipadyate  BVaky avasthāṃ pañcamīm āhur ṇyante tāṃ karmakartari nivṛttapreṣaṇād dhātoḥ prākṛte rthe ṇij ucyate  BVaky bravīti pacater arthaṃ sidhyatir na vinā ṇicā sa ṇyantaḥ pacater arthe prākṛte vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky keṣāṃ cid devadattāder vyāpāro yaḥ sakarmake sa vinā devadattādeḥ kaṭādiṣu vivakṣyate  BVaky nivṛttapreṣaṇaṃ karma svasya kartuḥ prayojakam preṣaṇāntarasaṃbandhe ṇyante lenābhidhīyate  BVaky sadṛśādiṣu yat karma kartṛtvaṃ pratipadyate āpattyāpādane tatra viṣayatvaṃ prati kriye  BVaky kutaś cid āhṛtya padam evaṃ ca parikalpane karmasthabhāvakatvaṃ syād darśanādyabhidhāyinām  BVaky viśeṣadarśanaṃ yatra kriyā tatra vyavasthitā kriyāvyavasthā tv anyeṣāṃ śabdair eva prakāśyate  BVaky kālabhāvādhvadeśānām antarbhūtakriyāntaraiḥ sarvair akarmakair yoge karmatvam upajāyate  BVaky ādhāratvam iva prāptās te punar dravyakarmasu kālādayo bhinnakakṣyaṃ yānti karmatvam uttaram  BVaky atas taiḥ karmabhir dhātur yukto dravyair akarmakaḥ lasya karmaṇi bhāve ca nimittatvāya kalpate  BVaky sarvaṃ cākathitaṃ karma bhinnakakṣyaṃ pratīyate dhātvarthoddeśabhedena tan nepsitatamaṃ kila  BVaky pradhānakarma kathitaṃ yat kriyāyāḥ prayojakam tatsiddhaye kriyāyuktam anyat tv akathitaṃ smṛtam  BVaky duhyādivan nayatyādau karmatvam akathāśrayam ākhyātānupayoge tu niyamāc cheṣa iṣyate  BVaky antarbhūtaṇijarthānāṃ duhyādīnāṃ ṇijantavat siddhaṃ pūrveṇa karmatvaṃ ṇijantaniyamas tathā  BVaky karaṇasya svakakṣyāyāṃ na prakarṣāśrayo yathā karmaṇo pi svakakṣyāyāṃ na syād atiśayas tathā  BVaky karmaṇas tv āptum iṣṭatva āśrite tiśayo yataḥ āśrīyate tato tyantaṃ bhedaḥ pūrveṇa karmaṇā  BVaky ṇijante ca yathā kartā sakriyaḥ san prayujyate na duhyādau tathā kartā niṣkriyo pi prayujyate  BVaky bhedavākyaṃ tu yan ṇyante nīduhiprakṛtau ca yat śabdāntaratvān naivāsti saṃsparśas tasya dhātunā  BVaky yathaivaikam apādānaṃ śāstre bhedena darśitam tathaikam eva karmāpi bhedena pratipāditam  BVaky nirvartyo vā vikāryo vā prāpyo vā sādhanāśrayaḥ kriyāṇām eva sādhyatvāt siddharūpo bhidhīyate  BVaky ahiteṣu yathā laulyāt kartur icchopajāyate viṣādiṣu bhayādibhyas tathaivāsau pravartate  BVaky pradhānetarayor yatra dravyasya kriyayoḥ pṛthak śaktir guṇāśrayā tatra pradhānam anurudhyate  BVaky pradhānaviṣayā śaktiḥ pratyayenābhidhīyate yadā guṇe tadā tadvad anuktāpi prakāśate  BVaky pacāv anuktaṃ yat karma ktvānte bhāvābhidhāyini bhujau śaktyantare py ukte tat taddharma prakāśate  BVaky iṣeś ca gamisaṃsparśād grāme yo lo vidhīyate tatreṣiṇaiva nirbhogaḥ kriyate gamikarmaṇaḥ  BVaky paktvā bhujyata ity atra keṣāṃ cin na vyapekṣate odanaṃ pacatiḥ so sāv anumānāt pratīyate  BVaky tathābhiniviśau karma yat tinante bhidhīyate ktvānte dhikaraṇatve pi na tatrecchanti saptamīm  BVaky yan nirvṛttāśrayaṃ karma prāpter apracitaṃ punaḥ bhakṣyādiviṣayāpattyā bhidyamānaṃ tad īpsitam  BVaky dhātor arthāntare vṛtter dhātvarthenopasaṃgrahāt prasiddher avivakṣātaḥ karmaṇo karmikā kriyā  BVaky bhedā ya ete catvāraḥ sāmānyena pradarśitāḥ te nimittādibhedena bhidyante bahudhā punaḥ  BVaky iti karmādhikāraḥatha karaṇādhikāraḥkriyāyāḥ pariniṣpattir yadvyāpārād anantaram vivakṣyate yadā tatra karaṇatvaṃ tadā smṛtam  BVaky vastutas tad anirdeśyaṃ na hi vastu vyavasthitam sthālyā pacyata ity eṣā vivakṣā dṛśyate yataḥ  BVaky karaṇeṣu tu saṃskāram ārabhante punaḥ punaḥ viniyogaviśeṣāṃś ca pradhānasya prasiddhaye  BVaky svakakṣyāsu prakarṣaś ca karaṇānāṃ na vidyate āśritātiśayatvaṃ tu paratas tatra lakṣaṇam  BVaky svātantrye pi prayoktāra ārād evopakurvate karaṇena hi sarveṣāṃ vyāpāro vyavadhīyate  BVaky kriyāsiddhau prakarṣo yaṃ nyagbhāvas tv eva kartari siddhau satyāṃ hi sāmānyaṃ sādhakatvaṃ prakṛṣyate  BVaky asyādīnāṃ tu kartṛtve taikṣṇyādi karaṇaṃ viduḥ taikṣṇyādīnāṃ svatantratve dvedhātmā vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky ātmabhede pi saty evam eko rthaḥ sa tathā sthitaḥ tadāśrayatvād bhede pi kartṛtvaṃ bādhakaṃ tataḥ  BVaky yathā ca saṃnidhānena karaṇatvaṃ pratīyate tathaivāsaṃnidhāne pi kriyāsiddheḥ pratīyate  BVaky stokasya vābhinirvṛtter anirvṛtteś ca tasya vā prasiddhiṃ karaṇatvasya stokādīnāṃ pracakṣate  BVaky dharmāṇāṃ tadvatā bhedād abhedāc ca viśiṣyate kriyāvadher avaccheda viśeṣād bhidyate yathā  BVaky iti karaṇādhikāraḥatha kartradhikāraḥprāg anyataḥ śaktilābhān nyagbhāvāpādanād api tadadhīnapravṛttitvāt pravṛttānāṃ nivartanāt  BVaky adṛṣṭatvāt pratinidheḥ praviveke ca darśanāt ārād apy upakāritve svātantryaṃ kartur ucyate  BVaky dharmair abhyuditaiḥ śabde niyamo na tu vastuni kartṛdharmavivakṣāyāṃ śabdāt kartā pratīyate  BVaky ekasya buddhyavasthābhir bhede ca parikalpite kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca karmatvaṃ copajāyate  BVaky utpatteḥ prāg asadbhāvo buddhyavasthānibandhanaḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ satānyena kartā bhavati janmanaḥ  BVaky kāraṇaṃ kāryabhāvena yadā vāvyavatiṣṭhate kāryaśabdaṃ tadā labdhvā kāryatvenopajāyate  BVaky yathāheḥ kuṇḍalībhāvo vyagrāṇāṃ vā samagratā tathaiva janmarūpatvaṃ satām eke pracakṣate  BVaky vibhaktayoni yat kāryaṃ kāraṇebhyaḥ pravartate svā jātir vyaktirūpeṇa tasyāpi vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky bhāveṣv eva padanyāsaḥ prajñāyā vāca eva vā nāstīty apy apade nāsti na ca sad bhidyate tataḥ  BVaky buddhiśabdau pravartete yathābhūteṣu vastuṣu teṣām anyena tattvena vyavahāro na vidyate  BVaky ākāśasya yathā bhedaś chāyāyāś calanaṃ yathā janmanāśāv abhede pi tathā kaiś cit prakalpitau  BVaky yathaivākāśanāstitvam asan mūrtinirūpitam tathaiva mūrtināstitvam asadākāśaniśrayam  BVaky yathā tadarthair vyāpāraiḥ kriyātmā vyapadiśyate abhedagrahaṇād eṣa kāryakāraṇayoḥ kramaḥ  BVaky vikāro janmanaḥ kartā prakṛtir veti saṃśaye bhidyate pratipattṛṇāṃ darśanaṃ lingadarśanaiḥ  BVaky kḷpi saṃpadyamāne yā caturthī sā vikārataḥ suvarṇapiṇḍe prakṛtau vacanaṃ kuṇḍalāśrayam  BVaky vākye saṃpadyateḥ kartā sanghaś cvyantasya kathyate vṛttau saṅghībhavantīti brāhmaṇānāṃ svatantratā  BVaky atvaṃ saṃpadyate yas tvaṃ na tasmin yuṣmadāśrayā pravṛttiḥ puruṣasyāsti prākṛtaḥ sa vidhīyate  BVaky pūrvāvasthām avijahat saṃspṛśan dharmam uttaram saṃmūrchita ivārthātmā jāyamāno bhidhīyate  BVaky savyāpārataraḥ kaś cit kva cid dharmaḥ pratīyate saṃsṛjyante ca bhāvānāṃ bhedavatyo pi śaktayaḥ  BVaky viparītārthavṛttitvaṃ puruṣasya viparyaye gamyeta sādhanaṃ hy atra savyāpāraṃ pratīyate  BVaky tvam anyo bhavasīty eṣā tatra syāt parikalpanā rājñi bhṛtyatvamāpanne yathā tadvad gatir bhavet  BVaky saṃbhāvanāt kriyāsiddhau kartṛtvena samāśritaḥ kriyāyām ātmasādhyāyāṃ sādhanānāṃ prayojakaḥ  BVaky prayogamātre nyagbhāvaṃ svātantryād eva niśritaḥ aviśiṣṭo bhavaty anyaiḥ svatantrair muktasaṃśayaiḥ  BVaky nimittebhyaḥ pravartante sarva eva svabhūtaye abhiprāyānurodho pi svārthasyaiva prasiddhaye  BVaky iti kartradhikāraḥatha hetvadhikāraḥpreṣaṇādhyeṣaṇe kurvaṃs tatsamarthāni cācaran kartaiva vihitāṃ śāstre hetusaṃjñāṃ prapadyate  BVaky dravyamātrasya tu praiṣe pṛcchyāder loḍ vidhīyate sakriyasya prayogas tu yadā sa viṣayo ṇicaḥ  BVaky guṇakriyāyāṃ svātantryāt preṣaṇe karmatāṃ gataḥ niyamāt karmasaṃjñāyāḥ svadharmeṇābhidhīyate  BVaky kriyāyāḥ prerakaṃ karma hetuḥ kartuḥ prayojakaḥ karmārthā ca kriyotpatti saṃskārapratipattibhiḥ  BVaky iti hetvadhikāraḥatha saṃpradānādhikāraḥanirākaraṇāt kartus tyāgāngaṃ karmaṇepsitam preraṇānumatibhyāṃ ca labhate saṃpradānatām  BVaky hetutve karmasaṃjñāyāṃ śeṣatve vāpi kārakam rucyarthādiṣu śāstreṇa saṃpradānākhyam ucyate  BVaky bhedasya ca vivakṣāyāṃ pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ kriyāṃ prati parasyāngasya karmatvān na kriyāgrahaṇaṃ kṛtam  BVaky kriyāṇāṃ samudāye tu yadaikatvaṃ vivakṣitam tadā karma kriyāyogāt svākhyayaivopacaryate  BVaky bhedābhedavivakṣā ca svabhāvena vyavasthitā tasmād gatyarthakarmatve vyabhicāro na dṛśyate  BVaky vikalpenaiva sarvatra saṃjñe syātām ubhe yadi ārambheṇa na yogasya pratyākhyānaṃ samaṃ bhavet  BVaky tyāgarūpaṃ prahātavye prāpye saṃsargadarśanam āsthitaṃ karma yat tatra dvairūpyaṃ bhajate kriyā  BVaky iti saṃpradānādhikāraḥathāpādānādhikāraḥnirdiṣṭaviṣayaṃ kiṃ cid upāttaviṣayaṃ tathā apekṣitakriyaṃ ceti tridhāpādānam ucyate  BVaky saṃyogabhedād bhinnātmā gamir eva bhramir yathā dhruvāvadhir apāyo pi samavetas tathādhruve  BVaky dravyasvabhāvo na dhrauvyam iti sūtre pratīyate apāyaviṣayaṃ dhrauvyaṃ yat tu tāvad vivakṣitam  BVaky saraṇe devadattasya dhrauvyaṃ pāte tu vājinaḥ āviṣṭaṃ yad apāyena tasyādhrauvyaṃ pracakṣate  BVaky ubhāv apy adhruvau meṣau yady apy ubhayakarmaje vibhāge pravibhakte tu kriye tatra vivakṣite  BVaky meṣāntarakriyāpekṣam avadhitvaṃ pṛthak pṛthak meṣayoḥ svakriyāpekṣaṃ kartṛtvaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak  BVaky abhedena kriyaikā tu dvisādhyā ced vivakṣitā meṣāv apāye kartārau yady anyo vidyate vadhiḥ  BVaky gatir vinā tv avadhinā nāpāya iti gamyate vṛkṣasya parṇaṃ patatīty evaṃ bhāṣye nidarśitam  BVaky bhedābhedau pṛthagbhāvaḥ sthitiś ceti virodhinaḥ yugapan na vivakṣyante sarve dharmā balāhake  BVaky dhanuṣā vidhyatīty atra vināpāyavivakṣayā karaṇatvaṃ yato nāsti tasmāt tad ubhayaṃ saha  BVaky ekaiva vā satī śaktir dvirūpā vyavatiṣṭhate nimittaṃ saṃjñayos tatra parayā bādhyate parā  BVaky nirdhāraṇe vibhakte yo bhītrādīnāṃ ca yo vidhiḥ upāttāpekṣitāpāyaḥ so budhapratipattaye  BVaky ity apādānādhikāraḥathādhikaraṇādhikāraḥkartṛkarmavyavahitām asākṣād dhārayat kriyām upakurvat kriyāsiddhau śāstre dhikaraṇaṃ smṛtam  BVaky upaśleṣasya cābhedas tilākāśakaṭādiṣu upakārās tu bhidyante saṃyogisamavāyinām  BVaky avināśo gurutvasya pratibandhe svatantratā digviśeṣād avaccheda ityādyā bhedahetavaḥ  BVaky ākāśam eva keṣāṃ cid deśabhedaprakalpanāt ādhāraśaktiḥ prathamā sarvasaṃyogināṃ matā  BVaky idam atreti bhāvānām abhāvān na prakalpate vyapadeśas tam ākāśa nimittaṃ saṃpracakṣate  BVaky kālāt kriyā vibhajyanta ākāśāt sarvamūrtayaḥ etāvāṃś caiva bhedo yam abhedopanibandhanaḥ  BVaky yady apy upavasir deśa viśeṣam anurudhyate śabdapravṛttidharmāt tu kālam evāvalambate  BVaky vasatāv aprayukte pi deśo dhikaraṇaṃ tataḥ aprayuktaṃ trirātrādi karma copavasau smṛtam  BVaky ity adhikaraṇādhikāraḥatha śeṣādhikāraḥsaṃbandhaḥ kārakebhyo nyaḥ kriyākārakapūrvakaḥ śrutāyām aśrutāyāṃ vā kriyāyāṃ so bhidhīyate  BVaky dviṣṭho py asau parārthatvād guṇeṣu vyatiricyate tatrābhidhīyamānaḥ san pradhāne py upayujyate  BVaky nimittaniyamaḥ śabdāt saṃbandhasya na gṛhyate karmapravacanīyais tu sa viśeṣo varudhyate  BVaky sādhanair vyapadiṣṭe ca śrūyamāṇakriye punaḥ proktā pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhī samāsasya nivṛttaye  BVaky niṣṭhāyāṃ karmaviṣayā ṣaṣthī ca pratiṣidhyate śeṣalakṣaṇayā ṣaṣṭhyā samāsastatra neṣyate  BVaky anyena vyapadiṣṭasya yasyānyatropajāyate vyatirekaḥ sa dharmau dvau labhate viṣayāntare  BVaky prādhānyaṃ svaguṇe labdhvā pradhāne yāti śeṣatām sahayoge svayoge taḥ pradhānatvaṃ na hīyate  BVaky iti śeṣādhikāraḥsiddhasyābhimukhībhāva mātraṃ saṃbodhanaṃ viduḥ prāptābhimukhyo hy arthātmā kriyāsu viniyujyate  BVaky saṃbodhanaṃ na vākyārtha iti pūrvebhya āgamaḥ uddeśena vibhaktyarthā vākyārthāt samapoddhṛtāḥ  BVaky vibhaktyarthe vyayībhāva vacanād avasīyatām anyo dravyād vibhaktyarthaḥ so vyayenābhidhīyate  BVaky dravyaṃ tu yad yathābhūtaṃ tad atyantaṃ tathā bhavet kriyāyoge pi tasyāsau dravyātmā nāpahīyate  BVaky tasmād yat karaṇaṃ dravyaṃ tat karma na punar bhavet sarvasya vānyathābhāvas tasya dravyātmano bhavet  BVaky  Kriyāsamuddeśayāvat siddham asiddhaṃ vā sādhyatvenābhidhīyate āśritakramarūpatvāt tat kriyeti pratiyate  BVaky kāryakāraṇabhāvena dhvanatīty āśritakramaḥ dhvaniḥ kramanivṛttau tu dhvanir ity eva kathyate  BVaky śvete śvetata ity etac chvetatvena prakāśate āśritakramarūpatvād abhidhānaṃ pravartate  BVaky guṇabhūtair avayavaiḥ samūhaḥ kramajanmanām buddhyā prakalpitābhedaḥ kriyeti vyapadiśyate  BVaky samūhaḥ sa tatbābhūtaḥ pratibhedam samūhisu samāpyate tato bhede kālabhedasya saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky kramāt sadasatāṃ teṣām ātmāno na samūhinām sadvastuviṣayair yānti saṃbandhaṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ  BVaky yathā gaur iti samghātaḥ sarvo nendriyagocaraḥ bhāgaśas tūpalabdhasya buddhau rūpaṃ nirūpyate  BVaky indriyair anyathāprāptau bhedāmśopanipātibhiḥ alātacakravad rūpaṃ kriyāṇāṃ parikalpyate  BVaky yathā ca bhāgāḥ pacater udakāsecanādayaḥ udakāsecanādināṃ jñeyā bhāgās tathāpare  BVaky yaś cāpakarṣaparyantam anuprāptaḥ pratīyate tatraikasmin kriyāśabdaḥ kevale na prayujyate  BVaky pūrvottarais tathā bhāgaiḥ samavasthāpitakramaḥ ekaḥ so py asadadhyāsād ākhyātair abhidhīyate  BVaky kālānupāti yad rūpaṃ tad astīty anugamyate paritas tu paricchinnaṃ bhāva ity eva kathyate  BVaky vyavahārasya siddhatvān na ceyaṃ guṇakalpanā upacāro hi mukhyasya saṃbhavād avatiṣṭhate  BVaky āhitottaraśaktitvāt pratyekaṃ vā samūhinaḥ anekarūpā lakṣyante kramavanta ivākramāḥ  BVaky anantaraṃ phalaṃ yasyāḥ kalpate tām kriyām viduḥ pradhānabhūtāṃ tādarthyād anyāsāṃ tu tadākhyatā  BVaky kriyāpravṛttau yo hetus tadarthaṃ yad viceṣṭitam anapekṣya prayuñjīta gacchatīty avadhārayan  BVaky satsu pratyayarūpo sau bhāvo yāvan na jāyate tāvat pareṣāṃ rūpeṇa sādhyaḥ sann abhidhīyate  BVaky siddhe tu sādhanākāṅkṣā kṛtārthatvān nivartate na kriyāvācināṃ tasmāt prayogas tatra vidyate  BVaky sa cāpūrvāparibhūta ekatvād akramātmakaḥ pūrvāparāṇāṃ dharmeṇa tadarthenānugamyate  BVaky asan nivartate tasmād yat sat tad upalabhyate tayoḥ sadasatoś cāsāv ātmaika iva gṛhyate  BVaky jātim anye kriyām āhur anekavyaktivartinīm asādhyā vyaktirūpeṇa sā sādhyevopalabhyate  BVaky ante yā vā kriyābhāge jātiḥ saiva kriyā smṛtā sā vyakter anuniṣpāde jāyamāneva gamyate  BVaky svavyāpāraviśiṣṭānām sattā vākartṛkarmanām kriyā vyāpārabhedeṣu sattā vā samavāyinī  BVaky antye vātmani yā sattā sā kriyā kaiś cid iṣyate bhāva eva hi dhātvartha ity avicchinna āgamaḥ  BVaky buddhiṃ tajjātim anye tu buddhisattām athāpare pratyastarūpāṃ bhāveṣu kriyeti pratijānate  BVaky āvirbhāvatirobhāvau janmanāśau tathāparaiḥ ṣaṭsu bhāvavikāreṣu kalpitau vyāvahārikau  BVaky tābhyāṃ sarvapravṛttīnām abhedenopasamgrahaḥ janmaivāśritasārūpyaṃ sthitir ity abhidhīyate  BVaky jāyamānān na janrnānyad vināśe py apadārthatā ato bhāvavikāreṣu sattaikā vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky pūrvabhāgas tu yaj jātāt taj janmety apadiśyate āśritakramarūpeṇa nimittatve vivakṣite  BVaky ākhyātaśabdair artho sāv evaṃbhūto bhidhīyate nāmaśabdāḥ pravartante saṃharanta iva kramam  BVaky phalaṃ phalāpadeśo vā vastu vā tadvirodhi yat tad anyad eva pūrveṣāṃ nāga ity apadiśyate  BVaky naivāsti naiva nāstīti vastuno grahanād vinā kalpate pararūpeṇa vastv anyad anugamyate  BVaky bhāvābhāvau ghaṭādinām aspṛśann api pāṇinā kaś cid vedāprakāśe pi prakāśe tata eva vā  BVaky vyāpi saukṣmyaṃ kva cid yāti kva cit saṃhanyate punaḥ akurvāṇo tha vā kiṃ cit svaśaktyaivaṃ prakāśate  BVaky sarvarūpasya tattvasya yat krameṇeva darśanam bhāgair iva prakḷptiś ca tāṃ kriyām apare viduḥ  BVaky sattā svaśaktiyogena sarvarūpā vyavasthitā sādhyā ca sādhanaṃ caiva phalaṃ bhoktā phalasya ca  BVaky kriyām anye tu manyante kva cid apy anapāśritām sādhanaikārthakāritve pravṛttim anapāyinīm  BVaky sāmānyabhūtā sā pūrvaṃ bhāgaśaḥ pravibhajyate tato vyāpārarūpeṇa sādhyeva vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky prakṛtiḥ sādhanānāṃ sā prathamaṃ tac ca kārakam vyāpārāṇāṃ tato nyatvam aparair upavarṇyate  BVaky bahūnāṃ saṃbhave rthānāṃ ke cid evopakārinaḥ saṃsarge kaś cid esāṃ tu prādhānyena pratīyate  BVaky sādhyatvāt tatra cākhyātair vyāpārāḥ siddhasādhanāḥ prādhānyenābhidhīyante phalenāpi pravartitāḥ  BVaky ekatvāvṛttibhāvābhyāṃ bhedābhedasamanvaye saṃkhyās tatropalabhyante saṃkhyeyāvayavakriyāḥ  BVaky siddhasyārthasya pākādeḥ kathaṃ sādhanayogitā sādhyatve vā tiṅantena kṛtāṃ bhedo na kaś cana  BVaky tatra kārakayogāyā yady ākhyātaṃ nibandhanam ṣaṣṭhvāḥ sā lena saṃbandhe vyudastā kartṛkarmanoḥ  BVaky ekābhidhāna eko rtho yugapac ca dvidharmabhāk na saṃbhavati siddhatve sa sādhyaḥ syāt kathaṃ punaḥ  BVaky etāvat sādhanaṃ sādhyam etāvad iti kalpanā śāstra eva na vākye sti vibhāgaḥ paramārthataḥ  BVaky ākhyātaśabde bhāgābhyāṃ sādhyasādhanavartitā prakalpitā yathā śāstre sa ghañādisv api kramaḥ  BVaky sādhyatvena kriyā tatra dhāturūpanibandhanā sattvabhāvas tu yas tasyāḥ sa ghañādinibandhanaḥ  BVaky bandhutābhedarūpeṇa bandhuśabde vyavasthitā samūho bandhvavasthā tu pratyayenābhidhīyate  BVaky tatra yam prati sādhyatvam asiddhā taṃ prati kriyā siddhā tu yasmin sādhyatvaṃ na tam eva punaḥ prati  BVaky rājñaḥ putrasya napteti na rājñi vyatiricyate putrasyārthaḥ pradhānatvaṃ na cāsya vinivartate  BVaky mṛgo dhāvati paśyeti sādhyasādhanarūpatā tathā viṣayabhedena saraṇasyopapadyate  BVaky lakṛtyaktakhalarthānāṃ tathāvyayakṛtām api rūḍhiniṣṭhāghañādinām dhātuḥ sādhyasya vācakaḥ  BVaky sādhyasyāpariniṣpatteḥ so yam ity anupagrahaḥ tiṅantair antareṇevam upamānaṃ tato na taiḥ  BVaky sādhanatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ ca tiṅkṣu saṃbandhināṃ yataḥ tenādhyāropa eva syād upamā tu na vidyate  BVaky nyūneṣu ca samāptārtham upamānaṃ vidhīyate kriyā caivāśraye sarvā tatra tatra samāpyate  BVaky yenaiva hetunā haṃsaḥ patatīty abhidhīyate ātau tasya samāptatvād upamārtho na vidyate  BVaky kriyāṇāṃ jātibhinnānāṃ sādṛśyaṃ nāvadhāryate siddheś ca prakrame sādhyam upamātum na śakyate  BVaky vanam vṛkṣā iti yathā bhedābhedavyapāśrayāt arthātmā bhidyate bhāve sa bāhyābhyantare kramaḥ  BVaky sāmānye bhāva ity atra yal liṅgam upalabhyate bhedānāṃ anumeyatvān na tat teṣu vivakṣyate  BVaky nirdeśe caritārthatvāl liṅgaṃ bhāve vivaksitam upamānavidhitvāc ca bhāvād anyat pacādisu  BVaky bhavatau yat pacādināṃ tāvad atropadiśyate na ca liṅgam pacādināṃ bhavatau samavasthitam  BVaky ekaś ca so rthaḥ sattākhyaḥ katham cit kaiś cid ucyate liṅgāni cāsya bhidyante pacirūpādibhedavat  BVaky ācāryo mātulaś ceti yathaiko vyapadiśyate sambandhibhedād arthātmā sa vidhiḥ paktibhāvayoḥ  BVaky  Kālasamuddeśaḥvyāpāravyatirekeṇa kālam eke pracakṣate nityam ekaṃ vibhu dravyaṃ parimāṇaṃ kriyāvatām  BVaky diṣṭiprasthasuvarṇādi mūrtibhedāya kalpate kriyābhedāya kālas tu saṃkhyā sarvasya bhedikā  BVaky utpattau ca sthitau caiva vināśe cāpi tadvatām nimittaṃ kālam evāhur vibhaktenātmanā sthitam  BVaky tam asya lokayantrasya sūtradhāraṃ pracakṣate pratibandhābhyanujñābhyāṃ tena viśvaṃ vibhajyate  BVaky yadi na pratibadhnīyāt pratibandhaṃ ca notsṛjet avasthā vyatikīryeran paurvāparyavinākṛtāḥ  BVaky tasyātmā bahudhā bhinno bhedair dharmāntarāśrayaiḥ na hi bhinnam abhinnaṃ vā vastu kiṃ cana vidyate  BVaky naiko na cāpy aneko sti na śuklo nāpi cāsitaḥ dravyātmā sa tu saṃsargād evaṃrūpaḥ prakāśate  BVaky saṃsargināṃ tu ye bhedā viśeṣās tasya te matāḥ sa bhinnas tair vyavasthānāṃ kālo bhedāya kalpate  BVaky viśiṣṭakālasaṃbandhād vṛttilābhaḥ prakalpate śaktīnāṃ saṃprayogasya hetutvenāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky janmābhivyaktiniyamāḥ prayogopanibandhanāḥ nityādhīnasthititvāc ca sthitir niyamapūrvikā  BVaky sthitasyānugrahas tais tair dharmaiḥ saṃsargibhis tataḥ pratibandhas tirobhāvaḥ prahāṇam iti cātmanaḥ  BVaky pratyavasthaṃ tu kālasya vyāpāro tra vyavasthitaḥ kāla eva hi viśvātmā vyāpāra iti kathyate  BVaky mūrtīnāṃ tena bhinnānām ācayāpacayāḥ pṛthak lakṣyante pariṇāmena sarvāsāṃ bhedayoginā  BVaky jalayantrabhramāveśa sadṛśībhiḥ pravṛttibhiḥ sa kalāḥ kalayan sarvāḥ kālākhyāṃ labhate vibhuḥ  BVaky pratibhaddhāś ca yās tena citrā viśvasya vṛttayaḥ tāḥ sa evānujānāti yathā tantuḥ śakuntikāḥ  BVaky viśiṣṭakālasaṃbandhāl labdhapākāsu śaktiṣu kriyābhivyajyate nityā prayogākhyena karmaṇā  BVaky jātiprayuktā tasyāṃ tu phalavyaktiḥ prajāyate kuto py adbhutayā vṛttyā śaktibhiḥ sā niyamyate  BVaky tatas tu samavāyākhyā śaktir bhedasya bādhikā ekatvam iva tā vyaktīr āpādayati kāraṇaiḥ  BVaky athāsmān niyamād ūrdhvaṃ jātayo yāḥ prayojikāḥ tāḥ sarvā vyaktim āyānti svacche chāyā ivāmbhasi  BVaky kāraṇānuvidhāyitvād atha kāraṇa pūrvakāḥ guṇās tatropajāyante svajātivyaktihetavaḥ  BVaky āśrayāṇāṃ ca nityatvam āśritānāṃ ca nityatā tā vyaktīr anugṛhṇāti sthitis tena prakalpate  BVaky anityasya yathotpāde pāratantryaṃ tathā sthitau vināśāyaiva tat śṛṣṭam asvādhīnasthitiṃ viduḥ  BVaky sthitaḥ saṃsargibhir bhāvaiḥ svakriyāsv anugṛhyate naiṣāṃ sattām anudgṛhya vṛttir janmavatāṃ smṛtā  BVaky jarākhyā kālaśaktir yā śaktyantaravirodhinī sā śaktīḥ pratibadhnāti jāyante ca virodhinaḥ  BVaky prayojakās tu ye bhāvāḥ sthitibhāgasya hetavaḥ tirobhavanti te sarve yata ātmā prahīyate  BVaky yathaivādbutayā vṛttyā niṣkramaṃ nirnibandhanam apadaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ tathāsyātmā prahīyate  BVaky kriyayor apavargiṇyor nānārthasamavetayoḥ saṃbandhinā vinaikena paricchedaḥ kathaṃ bhavet  BVaky yathā tulāyāṃ haste vā nānādravyavyavasthitam gurutvaṃ parimīyeta kālād evaṃ kriyāgatiḥ  BVaky jahāti sahavṛttāś ca kriyāḥ sa samavasthitāḥ vrīhir yathodakaṃ tena hāyanākhyāṃ prapadyate  BVaky pratibandhābhyanujñābhyāṃ vṛttir yā tasya śāsvatī tayā vibhajyamāno sau bhajate kramarūpatāṃ  BVaky kartṛbhedāt tadartheṣu pracayāpacayau gataḥ samatvaṃ viṣamatvaṃ vā sa ekaḥ pratipadyate  BVaky kriyābhedād yathaikasmiṃs takṣādyākhyā pravartate kriyābhedāt tathaikasminn ṛtvādyākhyopajāyate  BVaky ārambhaś ca kriyā caiva niṣṭhā cety abhidhīyate dharmāntarāṇām adhyāsa bhedāt sadasadātmanaḥ  BVaky yāvāṃś ca dvyaṇukādīnāṃ tāvān himavato py asau na hy ātmā kasya cid bhettuṃ pracetuṃ vāpi śakyate  BVaky anyais tu bhāvair anyeṣāṃ pracayaḥ parikalpyate śanair idam idaṃ kṣipram iti tena pratīyate  BVaky asataś ca kramo nāsti sa hi bhettuṃ na śakyate sato pi cātmatattvaṃ yat tat tathaivāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky kriyopādhiś ca san bhūta bhaviṣyadvartamānatāḥ ekādaśābhir ākārair vibhaktāḥ pratipadyate  BVaky bhūtaḥ pañcavidhas tatra bhaviṣyaṃś ca caturvidhaḥ vartamāno dvidhākhyāta ity ekādaśa kalpanāḥ  BVaky kāle nidhāya svaṃ rūpaṃ prajñayā yan nigṛhyate bhāvās tato nivartante tatra saṃkrāntaśaktayaḥ  BVaky bhāvināṃ caiva yad rūpaṃ tasya ca pratibimbakam sunirmṛṣṭa ivādarśe kāla evopapadyate  BVaky tṛṇaparṇalatādīni yathā sroto nukarṣati pravartayati kālo pi mātrā mātrāvatāṃ tathā  BVaky āviśyevānusaṃdhatte yathā gatimatāṃ gatīḥ vāyus tatraiva kālātmā vidhatte kramarūpatām  BVaky ayanapravibhāgaś ca gatīś ca jyotiṣāṃ dhruvā nivṛttiprabhavāś caiva bhūtānāṃ tannibandhanāḥ  BVaky mātrāṇāṃ pariṇāmā ye kālavṛttyanupātinaḥ nakṣatrākhyā pṛthak teṣu cihnamātraṃ tu tārakāḥ  BVaky rutair mṛgaśakuntānāṃ sthāvarāṇāṃ ca vṛttibhiḥ chāyādipariṇāmaiś ca ṛtudhāmā nirūpyate  BVaky nirbhāsopagamo yo yaṃ kramavān iva dṛśyate akramasyāpi viśvasya tat kālasya viceṣṭitam  BVaky dūrāntikavyavasthānam adhvādhikaraṇaṃ yathā cirakṣipravyavasthānaṃ kālādhikaraṇaṃ tathā  BVaky tasyābhinnasya kālasya vyavahāre kriyākṛtāḥ bhedā iva trayaḥ siddhā yāṃl loko nātivartate  BVaky ekasya śaktayas tisraḥ kālasya samavasthitāḥ yatsaṃbandhena bhāvānāṃ darśanādarśane satām  BVaky dvābhyāṃ sa kila śaktibhyāṃ bhāvānāṃ varaṇātmakaḥ śaktis tu vartamānākhyā bhāvarūpaprakāśinī  BVaky anāgatā janmaśakteḥ śaktir apratibandhikā atītākhyā tu yā śaktis tayā janma virudhyate  BVaky tamaḥprakāśavat tv ete trayo dhvāno vyavasthitāḥ akramās teṣu bhāvānāṃ kramaḥ samupalabhyate  BVaky dvau tu tatra tamorūpāv ekasyālokavat sthitiḥ atītam api keṣāṃ cit punar viparivartate  BVaky yugapad vartamānatvaṃ taddharmā pratipadyate keṣāṃ cid vartamānatvāc caiti tadvad atītatām  BVaky hetupakārād ākṣipto vartamānatvam āgataḥ śāntahetūpakāraḥ san punar nopaiti darśanam  BVaky dve eva kālasya vibhoḥ keṣāṃ cic chaktivartmanī karoti yābhyāṃ bhāvānām unmīlananimīlane  BVaky kalābhiḥ pṛthagarthābhiḥ pravibhaktaṃ svabhāvataḥ ke cid buddhyanusaṃhāra lakṣaṇaṃ taṃ pracakṣate  BVaky jñānānugataśaktiṃ vā bāhyaṃ vā satyataḥ sthitam kālātmānam anāśritya vyavahartuṃ na śakyate  BVaky tisro bhāvasya bhāvasya keṣāṃ cid bhāvaśaktayaḥ tābhiḥ svaśaktibhiḥ sarvaṃ sadaivāsti ca nāsti ca  BVaky sattvād avyatirekeṇa tās tisro pi vyavasthitāḥ kramas tās tadabhedāc ca sadasattvaṃ na bhidyate  BVaky darśanādarśanenaikaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaṃ tad eva tu adhvanām ekatā nāsti na ca kiṃ cin nivartate  BVaky śaktyātmadevatāpakṣair bhinnaṃ kālasya darśanam prathamaṃ tad avidyāyāṃ yad vidyāyāṃ na vidyate  BVaky abhede yadi kālasya hrasvadīrghaplutādiṣu dṛśyate bhedanirbhāsaḥ sa cirakṣiprabuddhivat  BVaky hrasvadīrghaplutāvṛttyā nālikāsalilādiṣu kathaṃ pracayayogaḥ syāt kalpanāmātrahetukaḥ  BVaky abhivyaktinimittasya pracayena pracīyate abhinnam api śabdasya tattvam apracayātmakam  BVaky evaṃ mātrāturīyasya bhedo dāśatayasya vā parimāṇavikalpena śabdātmani na vidyate  BVaky anuniṣpādikalpena ye ntarāla iva sthitāḥ śabdās te pratipattṝṇām upāyāḥ pratipattaye  BVaky viśiṣṭam avadhiṃ taṃ tam upādāya prakalpate kālaḥ kālavatām ekaḥ kṣaṇamāsartubhedabhāk  BVaky buddhyavagrahabhedāc ca vyavahārātmani sthitaḥ tāvān eva kṣaṇaḥ kālo yugamanvantarāṇi vā  BVaky pratibandhābhyanujñābhyāṃ nālikāvivarāśrite yad ambhasi prakṣaraṇaṃ tat kālasyaiva ceṣṭitam  BVaky alpe mahati vā chidre tatsaṃbandhe na bhidyate kālasya vṛttir ātmāpi tam evāsyānuvartate  BVaky ākrīḍa iva kālasya dṛśyate yaḥ svaśaktibhiḥ bahurūpasya bhāveṣu bahudhā tena bhidyate  BVaky tvacisārasya vā vṛddhiṃ tṛṇarājasya vā dadhat tāvat tadvṛddhiyogena kālatattvaṃ vikalpate  BVaky vyatikrame pi mātrāṇāṃ tasya nāsti vyatikramaḥ na gantṛgatibhedena mārgabhedo sti kaś cana  BVaky udayāstamayāvṛttyā jyotiṣāṃ lokasiddhayā kālasyāvyatipāte pi tāddharmyam iva lakṣyate  BVaky ādityagrahanakṣatra parispandam athāpare bhinnam āvṛttibhedena kālaṃ kālavido viduḥ  BVaky kriyāntarapariccheda pravṛttā yā kriyāṃ prati nirjñātaparimāṇā sā kāla ity abhidhīyate  BVaky jñāne rūpasya saṃkrāntir jñānenaivānusaṃhṛtiḥ ataḥ kriyāntarābhāve sā kriyā kāla iṣyate  BVaky bhūto ghaṭa itīyaṃ ca sattāyā eva bhūtatā bhūtā satteti sattāyāḥ sattā bhūtābhidhīyate  BVaky parato bhidyate sarvam ātmā tu na vikalpyate parvatādisthitis tasmāt pararūpeṇa bhidyate  BVaky prasiddhabhedā vyāpārā virūpāvayavakriyāḥ sāhacaryeṇa bhidyante sarūpāvayavakriyāḥ  BVaky vyavadhānam ivopaiti nivṛtta iva dṛśyate kriyāsamūho bhujyādir antarālapravṛttibhiḥ  BVaky na ca vicchinnarūpo pi so virāmān nivartate sarvaiva hi kriyānyena samkīrṇevopalabhyate  BVaky tadantarāladṛṣṭā vā sarvaivāvayavakriyā sādṛśyāt sati bhede tu tadaṅgatvena gṛhyate  BVaky sad asad vāpi vastu syāt tṛtīyaṃ nāsti kiṃ cana tena bhūtabhaviṣyantau muktvā madhyaṃ na vidyate  BVaky nirvṛttirūpam ekasya bhedābhāvān na kalpate sad asad vāpi tenaikaṃ kramarūpaṃ kathaṃ bhavet  BVaky bahūnāṃ cānavasthānād ekam evopalabhyate yathopalabdhi smaraṇaṃ tatra cāpy upapadyate  BVaky sadasadrūpam ekaṃ syād sarvasyaikatvakalpane nirvṛttirūpaṃ nirvṛtteḥ sāmānyam atha vā bhavet  BVaky kāryotpattau samarthaṃ vā svena dharmeṇa tat tathā ātmatattvena gṛhyeta sā cāsmin vartamānatā  BVaky kriyāprabandharūpaṃ yad adhyātmaṃ vinigṛhyate saṃkrāntarūpam ekatra tām āhur vartamānatām  BVaky kriyātipattir atyantaṃ kriyānutpattilakṣaṇā na ca bhūtam anutpannaṃ na bhaviṣyat tathāvidham  BVaky prāg viruddhakriyotpādān nirvṛtte vā virodhini vyāpāre vadhibhedena viṣayas tatra bhidyate  BVaky vyabhicāre nimittasya sādhutvaṃ na prakalpate bhāvy āsīd iti sūtreṇa tat kāle nyatra śiṣyate  BVaky svakāla eva sādhutve kālabhede gatiḥ katham vākyārthād atadartheṣu viśiṣṭatvaṃ na sidhyati  BVaky tadarthaś ced avayavo bhāvino bhūtatāgatiḥ na syād atyantabhūtatvam evaikaṃ tatra saṃbhavet  BVaky viśiṣṭakālatā pūrvaṃ tathāpi tu viśeṣaṇe āśrayāt so ntaraṅgatvāt tatra sādhur bhaviṣyati  BVaky āmiśra eva prakrāntaḥ sa padārthas tathāvidhaḥ kevalasya vimiśratvaṃ nitye rthe nopapadyate  BVaky śuddhe ca kāle vyākhyātam āmiśre na prasidhyati sādhutvam ayathākālaṃ tat sūtreṇopadiśyate  BVaky ākhyātapadavācye rthe nirvartyatvāt pradhānatā viśeṣaṇaṃ tadākṣepāt tatkāle vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky saṃpratyayānukāro vā śabdavyāpāra eva vā adhyasyate viruddhe rthe na ca tena virudhyate  BVaky bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyad ity etau pratyayau vartamānatām atyajantau prapadyete viruddhāśrayarūpatām  BVaky adhvano vartamānasya viṣayeṇa bhaviṣyatā bhāṣye bhaviṣyatkāleti kāryārthaṃ vyapadiśyate  BVaky icchā cikīrśatīty atra svakālam anurudhyate bhaviṣyati prakṛtyarthe tatkālaṃ nānurudhyate  BVaky āśāsyamānatantratvād āśaṃsāyāṃ viparyayaḥ prayoktṛdharmaḥ śabdārthe śabdair evānuśajyate  BVaky apchālibījasaṃyoge vartate niṣpadir yadā tatrāvayavavṛttitvād bhaviṣyatpratiṣedhanam  BVaky phalaprasavarūpe tu niṣpadau bhūtakālatā dharmāntareṣu tad rūpam adhyasya parikalpyate  BVaky upayukte nimittānāṃ vyāpāre phalasiddhaye tatra rūpaṃ yad adhyastaṃ tatkālaṃ tat pratīyate  BVaky niṣpattāv avadhiḥ kaś cit kaś cit prativivakṣitaḥ hetujanmavyapekṣātaḥ phalajanmeti cocyate  BVaky abahiḥsādhanādhīnā siddhir yatra vivakṣitā tat sādhanāntarābhāvāt siddham ity apadiśyate  BVaky tasmād avadhibhedena siddhā mukhyaiva bhūtatā anāgatatvam astitvaṃ hetudharmavyapekṣaṇe  BVaky satām indriyasaṃbandhāt saiva sattā viśiṣyate bhedena vyavahāro hi vastvantaranibandhanaḥ  BVaky astitvaṃ vastumātrasya buddhyā tu parigṛhyate yaḥ samāsādanād bhedaḥ sa tatra na vivakṣitaḥ  BVaky yogād vā strītvapuṃstvābhyāṃ na kiṃ cid avatiṣṭhate svasminn ātmani tatrānyad bhūtaṃ bhāvi ca kathyate  BVaky  Puruṣasamuddeśapratyaktā parabhāvaś cāpy upādhī kartṛkarmanoḥ tayoḥ śrutiviśeṣeṇa vācakau madhyamottamau  BVaky sad asad vāpi caitanyam etābhyām avagamyate caitanyabhāge prathamaḥ puruṣo na tu vartate  BVaky budhijānāticitibhiḥ prathame puruṣe sati samjñānārthair na caitanya syopayogaḥ prakāśyate  BVaky saṃbodhanārthaḥ sarvatra madhyame kaiś cid iṣyate tathā saṃbodhane sarvāṃ prathamāṃ yuṣmado viduḥ  BVaky saṃbodhanaṃ na loke sti vidhātavyena vastunā svāhendraśatrur vardhasva yathā rājā bhaveti ca  BVaky yuṣmadarthasya siddhatvān niyatā cādyudāttatā yuṣmadaḥ prathamāntasya paraś cen na padād asau  BVaky guṇapradhānatābhedaḥ puruśādiviparyayaḥ nirdeśaś cānyathā śāstre nityatvān na virudhyate  BVaky yathānirdeśam arthāḥ syur yesāṃ śāstraṃ vidhāyakam kim cit sāmānyam āśritya sthite tu pratipādanam  BVaky yo śve yaḥ pīṭha ity atra bhūtayor aśvapīṭhayoḥ yathopalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ tathārtheṣv anuśāsanam  BVaky  Saṃkhyāsamuddeśasaṃkhyāvān sattvabhūto rthaḥ sarva evābhidhīyate bhedābhedavibhāgo hi loke saṃkhyānibandhanaḥ  BVaky sa dharmo vyatirikto vā teṣāṃ ātmaiva vā tathā bhedahetutvam āśritya saṃkhyeti vyapadiśyate  BVaky samavetā paricchedye kva cid anyatra sā sthitā prakalpayati bhāvānāṃ saṃkhyā bhedaṃ tathātmanaḥ  BVaky paratve cāparatve ca bhede tulyā śrutir yathā saṃkhyāśabdābhidheyatvaṃ bhedahetos tathā guṇe  BVaky asvatantre svatantratvaṃ paradharmo yathā guṇe abhedye bhedyabhāvo pi dravyadharmas tathā guṇe  BVaky svabuddhyā tam apoddhṛtya loko py āgamam āśritaḥ svadharmād anyadharmeṇa vyācaṣṭe pratipattaye  BVaky paropakāratattvānāṃ svātantryenābhidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ sarvapadārthānā svadharmad viprakṛṣyate  BVaky yathaivāviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ na kiṃ cid avabhāsate tathā bhāvo py asaṃsṛṣṭo na kaś cid upalabhyate  BVaky bhedena tu samākhyātaṃ yal loko py anuvartate āgamāc chāstrasadṛśo vyavahāraḥ sa varṇyate  BVaky buddhau sthiteṣu teṣv evam adhyāropo na durlabhaḥ paradharmasya na hy atra sadasattvaṃ prayojakam  BVaky sāmānyeṣv api sāmānyaṃ viśeṣeṣu viśiṣṭatā saṃkhyāsu saṃkhyā liṅgeṣu liṅgam evaṃ prakalpate  BVaky ato dravyāśritāṃ saṃkhyām āhuḥ saṃsargavādinaḥ bhedābhedavyatīteṣu bhedābhedavidhāyinīm  BVaky ātmāntarānāṃ yenātmā tadrūpa iva lakṣyate atadrūpeṇa saṃsargāt sā nimittasarūpatā  BVaky saṃsṛṣṭeṣv api nirbhāge bhūteṣv arthakriyā yathā sattvādiṣu ca mātrāsu sarvāsv evaṃ pratīyate  BVaky dvitvādiyonir ekatvaṃ bhedās tatpūrvakā yataḥ vinā tena na saṃkhyānām anyāsām asti saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky ekatve buddhisahite nimittaṃ dvitvajanmani ekatvābhyāṃ samutpannam evaṃ vā tat pratīyate  BVaky ekatvasamudāyo vā sāpekṣe vā pṛthak pṛthak ekatve dvitvam ity evaṃ tayor dvivacanaṃ bhavet  BVaky eko pi guṇabhedena saṅgho bhedaṃ prakalpayet āśrayāśrayibhedo hi tadāśrayanibandhanaḥ  BVaky saṃkhyeyasaṅghasaṃkhyāna saṅghaḥ saṃkhyeti kathyate vimśatyādisu sānyasva dravyasaṅghasya bhedikā  BVaky ekaviṃśatisaṃkhvāvāṃ saṃkhyāntarasarūpayoḥ ekasyāṃ buddhyanāvṛttyābhāgayor iva kalpanā  BVaky asaṃkhyāsamudāyatvāt saṃkhyākāryaṃ vidhīyate samūhatve tu tan na syāt svāṅgādisamudāyavat  BVaky saṃkhyeyāntaratantrāsu yā saṃkhyāsu pravartate āvṛttivargasaṃkhyeyā tāṃ saṃkhyāṃ tādṛśīṃ viduḥ  BVaky na saṃkhyāyāṃ na saṃkhyeye dvau daśety asti saṃbhavaḥ bhedābhāvān na saṃkhyāyāṃ virodhān na tadāśraye  BVaky saṃkhyāyete daśadvargau dvidaśā iti saṃkhyayā tadrūpe vāpi saṃkhyeya āvṛttiḥ parigaṇyate  BVaky saṃkhyā nāma na saṃkhyāsti saṃjñaiṣeti yathocyate rūpaṃ na rūpam apy evaṃ samjñā sā hi sitādiṣu  BVaky saṃkhyānajātiyogāt tu saṃkhyā saṃkhyeti kathyate rūpatvajātiyogāc ca rūpe rūpam iti smṛtam  BVaky nimittam ekam ity atra vibhaktyā nābhidhīyate tadvatas tu yad ekatvaṃ vibhaktis tatra vartate  BVaky ekasya pracayo dṛṣṭaḥ samūhaś ca dvayos tathā nimittavyatirekeṇa saṃkhyānyā bhedikā tataḥ  BVaky tad ekam api caikatvaṃ vibhaktiśravaṇād ṛte nocyate tena śabdena vibhaktyā tu sahocyate  BVaky anvayavyatirekau ca yadi syād vacanāntaram syātām asati tasmimś ca prakṛtyartho na kalpyate  BVaky ekatvam eka ity atra śuddhadravyaviśeṣaṇam saguṇas tu prakṛtyartho vibhaktyarthena bhidyate  BVaky dvyekayor iti nirdeśāt saṃkhyāmātre pi saṃbhavaḥ ekādīnāṃ prasiddhyā tu saṃkhyeyārthatvam ucyate  BVaky  Upagrahasamuddeśaya ātmanepadād bhedaḥ kva cid arthasya gamyate anyataś cāpi lādeśān manyante tam upagraham  BVaky kva cit sādhanam evāsau kva cit tasya viśeṣaṇam sādhanaṃ tatra karmādi vyaktavāco viśeṣaṇam  BVaky kriyā viṣayabhedena jīvikādiṣu bhidyate lādeśaiḥ sa kriyābhedo vākyeṣv api niyamyate  BVaky dhātvarthas tadviśeṣaś cāpy uktaḥ kva cid upagrahaḥ dhātvartho gandhanādiḥ syād vyatihāro viśeṣaṇam  BVaky kriyāpravṛttāv ākhyātā kaiś cit svārthaparārthatā asati vā sati vāpi vivakṣitanibandhanā  BVaky kesāṃ cit kartrabhiprāye ṇicā saha vikalpate ātmanepadam anyesāṃ tadarthā prakṛtir yathā  BVaky krīṇīṣva vapate dhatte cinoti cinute pi ca āptaprayogā dṛśyante yeṣu ṇyartho bhidhīyate  BVaky saṃvidhānaṃ pacādināṃ kva cid arthaḥ pratīyate tannimittā yathānyāpi kriyādhiśrayaṇādikā  BVaky kartrabhiprāyatā sūtre kriyābhedopalakṣaṇam tathābhūtā kriyā yā hi tatkartā phalabhāg yataḥ  BVaky yathopalakṣyate kālas tārakādarśanādibhiḥ tathā phalaviśeṣeṇa kriyābhedo nidarśyate  BVaky kriyāviśeṣavacane sāmarthyam uparudhyate kesāṃ cid anye tu kṛtāḥ svariteto ñitas tathā  BVaky anubandhaś ca siddhe rthe smṛtyartham anuṣajyate tulyārtheṣv api cāvaśyaṃ na sarveṣv ekadharmatā  BVaky dṛśīkṣyoḥ sadṛśe py arthe nābhedaḥ pratipūrvayoḥ ṇyarthopādāyinas tasmān na tulyārthāḥ pacādibhiḥ  BVaky umbhyarthe vartamānasya karoter bhinnadharmaṇaḥ ṇyarthopādāyitā tasmān niyatāḥ śabdaśaktayaḥ  BVaky tathā hy anuprayogasya karoter ātmanepade pūrvavadgrahaṇaṃ prāpte svaritaṃ samupasthitam  BVaky ekatve pi kriyākhyāte sādhanāśrayasaṃkhyayā bhidyate na tu liṅgākhyo bhedas tatra tadāśritaḥ  BVaky tasmād avasthite py arthe kasya cit pratibadhyate śabdasya śaktiḥ sa tv eṣa śāstre nvākhyāyate vidhiḥ  BVaky yasyārthasya prasiddhyartham ārabhyante pacādayaḥ tat pradhānaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ na lābhādi prayojanam  BVaky yatrobhau svāmidāsau tu prārabhete saha kriyām yugapad dharmabhedena dhātus tatra na vartate  BVaky yatra pratividhānārthaḥ pacis tatrātmanepadam parasmaipadam anyatra saṃskārādyabhidhāyini  BVaky saṃvidhātuś ca sāṃnidhyād dāse dharmo nusajyate plakṣaśabdasya sāṃnidhyān nyagrodhe plakṣatā yathā  BVaky puroḍāśābhidhānaṃ ca dhānādiṣu yathā sthitam chattriṇā cābhisaṃbandhāc chattriśabdābhidheyatā  BVaky arthāt pratītam anyonyaṃ pārārthyam avivakṣitam ity ayaṃ śeṣaviṣayaḥ kaiś cid atrānuvarṇyate  BVaky atha pratividhātā yo halaiḥ kṛṣati pañcabhiḥ bhāṣye nodāhṛtaṃ kasmāt prāptaṃ tatrātmanepadam  BVaky pratītatvāt tadarthasya śeṣatvaṃ yadi kalpyate na syāt prāptavibhāṣāsau svaritetāṃ nivartikā  BVaky śuddhe tu saṃvidhānārthe kaiś cid atreṣyate kṛṣiḥ taddharmā yajir ity evaṃ na syāt tatrātmanepadam  BVaky atra tūpapadenāyam arthabhedaḥ pratīyate prāpte vibhāṣā kriyate tasmān nātrātmanepadam  BVaky  Liṅgasamuddeśastanakeśādisaṃbandho viśiṣṭā vā stanādayaḥ tadupavyañjanā jātir guṇāvasthā guṇās tathā  BVaky śabdopajanito rthātmā śabdasaṃskāra ity api liṅgānāṃ liṅgatattvajñair vikalpāḥ sapta darśitāḥ  BVaky upādānavikalpāś ca liṅgānāṃ sapta varṇitāḥ vikalpasaṃniyogābhyāṃ ye śabdeṣu vyavasthitāḥ  BVaky tisro jātaya evaitāḥ kesāṃ cit samavasthitāḥ aviruddhā viruddhābhir gomahiṣyādijātibhiḥ  BVaky hastinyāṃ vaḍavāyāṃ ca strīti buddheḥ samanvayaḥ atas tāṃ jātim icchanti dravyādisamavāyinīm  BVaky paratantrasya yal liṅgam apoddhāre vivakṣite tatrāsau śabdasaṃskāraḥ śabdair eva vyapāśritaḥ  BVaky buddhyā kalpitarūpeṣu liṅgeṣv api ca saṃbhavaḥ strītvādīnāṃ vyavasthā hi sā liṅgair vyapadiśyate  BVaky yathā salilanirbhāsā mṛgatṛṣṇāsu jāyate jalopalabdhyanuguṇād bījād buddhir jale sati  BVaky tathaivāvyapadeśyebhyo hetubhyas tārakādiṣu mukhyebhya iva liṅgebhyo bhedā loke vyavasthitāḥ  BVaky vyakteṣu vyaktarūpāṇāṃ stanādīnāṃ tu darśanāt avyaktavyañjanāvyakter jātir na parikalpyate  BVaky astitvaṃ ca pratijñāya sadādarśanam icchataḥ atyantādarśane na syād asattvaṃ prati niścayaḥ  BVaky na cālam anumānāya śabdo darśanapūrvakaḥ siddhe hi darśane kiṃ syād anumānaprayojanam  BVaky āvirbhāvas tirobhāvaḥ sthitiś cety anapāyinaḥ dharmā mūrtiṣu sarvāsu liṅgatvenānudarśitāḥ  BVaky sarvamūrtyātmabhūtānāṃ śabdādināṃ guṇe guṇe trayaḥ sattvādidharmās te sarvatra samavasthitāḥ  BVaky rūpasya cātmamātrānāṃ śuklādināṃ pratikṣaṇam kā cit pralīyate kā cit kathaṃ cid abhivardhate  BVaky kvathitodakavac caiṣām anavasthitavṛttitā ajasraṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāṣya evopavarṇitā  BVaky pravṛtter ekarūpatvaṃ sāmyaṃ vā sthitir ucyate avirbhāvatirobhāva pravṛttyā vāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky guṇā ity eva buddher vā nimittatvaṃ sthitir matā sthiteś ca sarvaliṅgānāṃ sarvanāmatvam ucyate  BVaky sthiteṣu sarvaliṅgeṣu vivakṣāniyamāśrayaḥ kasya cic chabdasaṃskāre vyāpāraḥ kva cid iṣyate  BVaky saṃnidhāne nimittānāṃ kiṃ cid eva pravartakam yathā takṣādiśabdānāṃ lingeṣu niyamas tathā  BVaky bhāvatattvadṛśaḥ śiṣṭāḥ śabdārtheṣu vyavasthitāḥ yad yad dharme ṅgatām eti liṅgaṃ tat tat pracakṣate  BVaky svarabhedād yathā śabdāḥ sādhavo viṣayāntare liṅgabhedāt tathā siddhāt sādhutvam anugamyate  BVaky prayogo viprayogaś ca loke yatropalabhyate śāstram ārabhyate tatra na prayogāviparyaye  BVaky upādhibhedād artheṣu guṇadharmasya kasya cit nimittabhāvaḥ sādhutve vivakṣā ca vyavasthitā  BVaky himāraṇye mahattvena yukte strītvam avasthitam hrasvopādhiviśiṣṭāyāḥ kuṭyāḥ prasavayogitā  BVaky śabdāntarānāṃ bhinne rtha upāyāḥ pratipattaye ekatām iva niścitya laghvartham upadarśitāḥ  BVaky utpattiḥ prasavo nyeṣāṃ nāśaḥ saṃstyānam ity api ātmarūpaṃ tu bhāvānāṃ sthitir ity apadiśyate  BVaky dṛṣṭaṃ nimittaṃ kesāṃ cij jātyādivad avasthitam dṛṣṭavac chabdasaṃskāra mātraṃ tu parikalpitam  BVaky yathā prasiddhe py ekatve nānātvābhiniveśinaḥ nānātvaṃ janayantīva śabdā liṅge pi sa kramaḥ  BVaky idaṃ veyam ayaṃ veti śabdasaṃskāramātrakam nimittadarśanād arthe kaiś cit sarvatra varṇyate  BVaky nāvaśyaṃ viṣayatvena nimittaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate indriyādi yathādṛṣṭaṃ bhedahetus tad iṣyate  BVaky  Vṛttisamuddeśakutsāpraśaṃsātiśayaiḥ samāptārthaṃ tu yujyate padaṃ svārthādayaḥ sarve yasmāt kutsādihetavaḥ  BVaky devadattādikutsāyāṃ vartate kutsitaśrutiḥ kutsitasthā tu yā kutsā tadarthaḥ ko vidhīyate  BVaky prakṛṣṭa iti śuklādi prakarṣasyābhidhāyakaḥ prakṛṣṭasya prakarṣe tu tarabādir vidhīyate  BVaky kutsitatvena kutsyo vā na samyag vāpi kutsitaḥ svaśabdābhihite kena viśiṣṭo rthaḥ pratīyate  BVaky na ca sāṃpratikī kutsā bhedābhāvāt pratīyate pūjyate kutsitatvena praśastatvena kutsyate  BVaky viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ padayor upajāyate na prātipadikārthaś ca tatraiva vyatiricyate  BVaky viśeṣyaṃ syād anirjñātaṃ nirjñāto rtho viśeṣaṇam parārthatvena śeṣatvaṃ sarveṣām upakāriṇām  BVaky vibhaktibhedo niyamād guṇaguṇyabhidhāyinoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasya prasiddhir dravyaśabdayoḥ  BVaky dravye nirjñātajātīye kṛṣṇaśabdaḥ prayujyate anirjñātaguṇe caivaṃ tilaśabdaḥ pravartate  BVaky sāmānyānām asaṃbandhāt tau viśeṣe vyavasthitau rūpābhedād viśeṣaṃ tam abhivyaṅktuṃ na śaknutaḥ  BVaky tāv eva saṃnipatitau bhedena pratipādane avacchedam ivādhāya saṃśayaṃ vyapakarṣataḥ  BVaky dravyātmā guṇasaṃsarga bhedād āśrīyate pṛthak jātisaṃbandhabhedāc ca dvitīya iva gṛhyate  BVaky nimittair abhisaṃbandhād yā nimittasarūpatā tayaikasyāpi nānātvaṃ rūpabhedāt prakalpate  BVaky dravyāvasthā tṛtīyā tu yasyāṃ saṃsṛjyate dvayam tayor avasthayor bhedād āśrayatve niyujyate  BVaky buddhyaikaṃ bhidyate bhinnam ekatvaṃ copagacchati buddhyāvasthā vibhajyante sā hy arthasya vidhāyikā  BVaky vyapadeśivad ekasmin buddhyā nānātvakalpanā tayā kalpitabhedaḥ sann arthātmā vyapadiśyate  BVaky kriyābhedena dṛṣṭānām aśmādīnāṃ punaḥ punaḥ kiṃ cid darśanam anyena darśanenāpadiśyate  BVaky prayogabhedād dhātūnāṃ prakalpya bahurūpatām bhedābhedāv upādāya kva cid ekāctvam ucyate  BVaky anvayavyatirekābhyām arthavān parikalpitaḥ eko dhātvarthavigamād varṇatvenopacaryate  BVaky dravyātmānas trayas tasmād buddhau nānā vyavasthitāḥ āśrayāśrayidharmeṇety ayaṃ pūrvebhya āgamaḥ  BVaky sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca śabdayoḥ kaiś cid iṣyate viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvam eva ca  BVaky keṣāṃ cij jātiguṇayor ekārthasamavetayoḥ vṛttiḥ kṛṣṇatileṣv iṣṭā śabde dravyābhidhāyini  BVaky saṃs tu rūparasādinām āśrayo nābhidhīyate dravyābhidhānena vinā tatas te dvandvabhāvinaḥ  BVaky dravyābhidhāyī kṛṣṇādir ākāṅkṣāvān pravartate nimittānuvidhāyitvāt tat tilādau na vidyate  BVaky evaṃ jātimati dravye pratyāsanne kriyāṃ prati guṇadharma guṇāviṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ bhedāya kalpate  BVaky guṇamātrābhidhāyitvaṃ ke cid icchanti vṛttiṣu ajāśvādiṣu saṃbandhād rūḍhīnām iva rūḍhibhiḥ  BVaky tile pūrvam upātte vā tatraiva matub iṣyate sa ca dharmaḥ samāseṣu guṇas tasmād viśeṣaṇam  BVaky paṭvīmṛdvyoḥ samāse tu yady apy ekārthavṛttitā bhinnam atrādhikaraṇaṃ prāg vṛttes tac ca gṛhyate  BVaky anusyūteva bhedābhyām ekā prakhyopajāyate yadā sahavivakṣāṃ tām āhur dvandvaikaśeṣayoḥ  BVaky itaretarayogas tu bhinnasaṅghābhidhāyinām pratyekaṃ ca samūho sau samūhiṣu samāpyate  BVaky vyāpārasamudāyasya yathādhiśrayaṇādiṣu pratyekaṃ jātivad vṛttis tathā dvandvapadeṣv api  BVaky śauṇḍārdharcapuroḍāśa cchattriṇo tra nidarśanam te viṣṇumitrā iti ca bhinneṣu sahacāriṣu  BVaky arthāntarābhidhāyitvaṃ tathārthāntaravartinām yābhyāṃ caikam anekārthaṃ tābhyām evāparaṃ padam  BVaky samudāyāntaratvāc ca tādṛśo rtho na laukikaḥ anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śāstrārtho pi na dṛśyate  BVaky duḥkhā durupapādā ca tasmād bhāṣye py udāhṛtā yugapadvācitā sā tu vyavahārārtham āśritā  BVaky samudāyam upakramya padaṃ tasyāṃ prayujyate vibhāgena samākhyāne tatas tad dvyartham ucyate  BVaky vākye pi niyatā dharmāḥ ke cid vṛttau dvayos tathā te tv abhedena sāmarthya mātra evopavarṇitāḥ  BVaky vṛttau viśeṣavṛttitvād bhede sāmānyavācitā upamānasamāsādau śyāmādīnām udāhṛtā  BVaky vṛttir anyapadārthe yā tasyā vākyeṣv asaṃbhavaḥ cārthe dvandvapadānāṃ ca bhede vṛttir na vidyate  BVaky bhede sati nirādīnāṃ krāntādyartheṣv asaṃbhavaḥ prāg vṛtter jātivācitvaṃ na ca gaurakharādiṣu  BVaky krīḍāyā jīvikāyāś ca vākyenāvacanāt tathā na nityagrahaṇaṃ yuktaṃ kauṭilye yaṅvidhau yathā  BVaky nirdhāraṇādiviṣaye vyapekṣaiva yataḥ sthitā samāsapratiṣedhānāṃ tato nāsti prayojanam  BVaky vidhibhiḥ pratiṣedhaiś ca bhedābhedanidarśanam kṛtaṃ dvandvaikavadbhāve saṅghavṛttyupadeśavat  BVaky sāmarthyam aviśeṣoktam api lokavyavasthayā vṛttyavṛttyoḥ prayogajñair vibhaktaṃ pratipattṛbhiḥ  BVaky arthasya vinivṛttatvāl lugādi na virudhyate ekārthībhāva evātaḥ samāsākhyā vidhīyate  BVaky vyavasthitavibhāṣā ca sāmānye kaiś cid iṣyate tathā vākyaṃ vyapekṣāyāṃ samāso nyatra śiṣyate  BVaky tulyaśrutitvāt tattve pi rājādīnām upāśrite vṛttau viśeṣaṇākāṅkṣā gamakatvān nivartate  BVaky saṃbandhiśabdaḥ sāpekṣo nityaṃ sarvaḥ prayujyate svārthavat sā vyapekṣāsya vṛttāv api na hīyate  BVaky samudāyena saṃbandho yesāṃ gurukulādinā saṃspṛśyāvayavāṃs te pi yujyante tadvatā saha  BVaky abudhān praty upāyāś ca vicitrāḥ pratipattaye śabdāntaratvād atyanta bhedo vākyasamāsayoḥ  BVaky asamāse samāse ca gorathādiṣv adarśanāt yuktādināṃ na śāstreṇa nivṛttyanugamaḥ kṛtaḥ  BVaky śabdāntaratvād yuktādiḥ kva cid vākye prayujyate praparṇaprapalāśādau gataśabdaś ca vṛttiṣu  BVaky viśeṣaṇaviśesyatvaṃ kaiś cid ekas tathāśrayaḥ upāye tattvadarśitvād iṣyate vṛttivākyayoḥ  BVaky padaṃ yathaiva vṛkṣādi viśiṣṭe rthe vyavasthitam nīlotpalādy api tathā bhāgābhyāṃ vartate vinā  BVaky śrotriyakṣetriyādināṃ na ca vāsiṣṭhagārgyavat bhedena pratyayo loke tulyarūpāsamanvayāt  BVaky saptaparṇādivad bhedo na vṛttau vidyate kva cit rūḍhyarūḍhivibhāgo pi kriyate pratipattaye  BVaky yā sāmānyāśrayā saṃjñā viśeṣaviṣayā ca yā bahulagrahaṇān nāsti pravṛttir ubhayos tayoḥ  BVaky susūkṣmajaṭakeśādau samāso vayave yadi syāt syāt tatrāntaraṅgatvād bādhako vayavasvaraḥ  BVaky samudāyasya vṛttau ca naikadeśo vibhāṣyate bheda eva vibhāṣāyā niyato viṣayo yataḥ  BVaky yataś cāviṣayaḥ so syās tasmān nāsty akṛtārthatā abhedaprakrame tyantaṃ bhedānām apasāraṇāt  BVaky mahākaṣṭaśritety evaṃ na syād bhedaḥ padatraye vṛttāv avayavasyāttvaṃ yasmān na pratiṣidhyate  BVaky mahāraṇyam atīte tu tripadād bhidyate svaraḥ yasmāt tatrāntaraṅgatvād bādhako vayavasvaraḥ  BVaky satiśiṣṭabaliyastvāt thāthādisvara eva tu dvipade tena yagapat tritayaṃ na samasyate  BVaky yeṣām apūjyamānatvaṃ parārthānugamātmake viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam api teṣāṃ na kalpate  BVaky viśeṣaḥ śrūyamāṇo pi pradhāneṣu guṇeṣu vā śabdāntaratvād vākye tu vṛttau nityaṃ na vidyate  BVaky viśeṣakarmasaṃbandhe nirbhukte pi kṛtādibhiḥ viśeṣanirapekṣo nyaḥ kṛtaśabdaḥ pravartate  BVaky akarmakatve saty evaṃ ktāntaṃ bhāvābhidhāyi tat tataḥ kriyāvatā kartrā yogo bhavati karmaṇām  BVaky avigrahā gatādisthā yathā grāmādikarmabhiḥ saṃbadhyate kriyā tadvat kṛtapūrvyādiṣu sthitā  BVaky muṇḍisūtrvādayo sadbhir bhāgair anugatā iva vibhaktāḥ kalpitātmāno dhātavaḥ kuṭṭicarcivat  BVaky putrīyatau na putro sti viśeṣecchā tu tādṛśī vinaiva putrānugamād yā putre vyavatiṣṭhate  BVaky prāṇair vinā yathā dhārir jīvatau prāṇakarmakaḥ na cātra dhārir na prāṇā jīvatis tu kriyāntaram  BVaky tathā vineṣiputrābhyāṃ putrīyāyāṃ kriyāntaram anvākhyānāya bhedās tu sadṛśāḥ pratipādakāḥ  BVaky ākṣepāc ca prayogena viṣayāntaravartinā sad apīcchākyacaḥ karma vākya eva prayujyate  BVaky prasiddhena hṛtaḥ śabdo bhāvagarhābhidhāyinā abhyāse tulyarūpatvān na yaṅantaḥ prayujyate  BVaky śabdā yathā vibhajyante bhāgair iva vikalpitaiḥ anvākhyeyās tathā śāstram atidūre vyavasthitam  BVaky arthasyānugamaṃ kaṃ cid dṛṣṭvaiva parikalpitam padaṃ vākye pade dhātur dhātau bhāgaś ca muṇḍivat  BVaky aviprayogaḥ sādhutve vyutpattir anavasthitā upāyān pratipattīnāṃ nābhimanyeta satyataḥ  BVaky yathaiva ḍitthe davatiḥ pācake pacatis tathā ḍayatiś ca paciś caiva dvāv apy etāv alaukikau  BVaky prakṛtipratyayāv ūhyau padāt tābhyāṃ padaṃ tathā anubandhasvarādibhyaḥ śiṣṭaiḥ śāstraṃ na tān prati  BVaky śāstradṛṣṭis tu śāstrasya prāptimātre py aniścite yujyate pratyavāyena śāstraṃ cakṣur apaśyatām  BVaky arthāntarābhidhānāc ca paurvāparyaṃ na bhidyate rājadantāhitāgnyādi rājāśvādiṣu sarvathā  BVaky vinaiva pratyayair vṛttau ye bhinnārthābhidhāyinaḥ gargādayo lukā teṣāṃ sādhutvam anugamyate  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhāt pratyayena vinā yadi bhṛgvādayaḥ prayujyeran nāpatye niyamo bhavet  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhe liṅgopavyañjanād ṛte praṣṭhādiṣu na jāyaiva niyamena pratīyate  BVaky mānameyābhisaṃbandha viśeṣe ṅgīkṛte tathā prasthādīnām asādhutvaṃ taddhitena vinā bhavet  BVaky taddhito yogabhedena vākyaṃ vā syād vibhāṣitam parimāṇādhike tatra prathamā śiṣyate punaḥ  BVaky vyatiriktasya sādhutve tad eva ca nidarśanam yujyate ṅgīkṛtādhikyaṃ tat sarvābhir vibhaktibhiḥ  BVaky śuklādiṣu matublopo vyatirekasya darśanāt asādhutvanivṛttyarthaṃ sādhavas te bidādivat  BVaky viśeṣaṇād viśeṣye rthe tadbhāvābhyuccaye sati punaś ca pratisaṃhāre vṛttim eke pracakṣate  BVaky nimitte pratyayaḥ pūrvo nānuprāpto nimittinā nimittavati buddheś ca na nimittasarūpatā  BVaky saṃskārasahitāj jñānān nopaślesaḥ smṛter api vyāpāre tannimittānāṃ na grāhyaṃ syāt tathā sthitam  BVaky antaḥkaraṇavṛttau ca vyarthā bāhyārthakalpanā tasmād anupakāre vā grāhyaṃ vā na tathā sthitam  BVaky anusyūteva saṃsṛṣṭair arthe buddhiḥ pravartate vyākhyātāro vibhajyārthāṃs tān bhedena pracakṣate  BVaky tadātmany avibhakte ca buddhyantaram upāśritāḥ vibhāgam iva manyante viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ  BVaky abudhān prati vṛttiṃ ca vartayantaḥ prakalpitām āhuḥ parārthavacane tyāgābhyuccayadharmatām  BVaky anvayād gamyate so rtho virodhī vā nivartate dvyartham arthāntare vāpi tatrāhur upasarjanam  BVaky upāyamātraṃ nānātvaṃ samūhas tv eka eva saḥ vikalpābhyuccayābhyāṃ vā bhedasaṃsargakalpanā  BVaky vṛttiṃ vartayatām evam abudhapratipattaye bhinnāḥ saṃbodhanopāyāḥ puruṣeṣv anavasthitāḥ  BVaky vācikā dyotikā vāpi saṃkhyānāṃ vā vibhaktayaḥ tadrūpe vayave vṛttau saṃkhyābhedo nivartate  BVaky abhedaikatvasaṃkhyā vā tatrānyaivopajāyate saṃsargarupaṃ saiṃkhyānām avibhaktaṃ tad ucyate  BVaky yathauṣadhirasāḥ sarve madhuny āhitaśaktayaḥ avibhāgena vartante tāṃ saṃkhyāṃ tādṛśīṃ viduḥ  BVaky bhedānāṃ vā parityāgāt saṃkhyātmā sa tathāvidhaḥ vyāpārāj jātibhāgasya bhedāpohena vartate  BVaky agṛhītaviśeṣeṇa yathā rūpeṇa rūpavān prakhyāyate na śuklādi bhedarūpas tu gṛhyate  BVaky bhedarūpasamāveśe tathā saty avivakṣite bhāgaḥ prakāśitaḥ kaś cic chāstre ṅgatvena gṛhyate  BVaky saṃkḥyāsāmānyarūpeṇa tadā so mśaḥ pratīyate arthasyānekaśaktitve śabdair niyataśaktibhiḥ  BVaky avyayānāṃ ca yo dharmo yaś ca bhedavatāṃ kramaḥ abhinnavyapadeśārham antarālaṃ tad etayoḥ  BVaky alukaś caikavadbhāvas tasmin sati na śiṣyate sa ca goṣucarādīnāṃ dharmo sti vacanāntare  BVaky jātau dvivacanābhāvāt tad vṛttiṣu na vidyate pratyākhyāne tu yogasya dravye goṣucarādayaḥ  BVaky āśrayād bhedavattāyāḥ sarvabhedasamanvayaḥ dravyābhidhānapakṣo pi jātyākhyāyāṃ na vidyate  BVaky sarvadravyagatiś caivam ekaśeṣaś ca nocyate pratyākhyāte nyathā sūtre bhinnadravyagatir bhavet  BVaky vṛttau yo yuktavadbhāvo varaṇādiṣu śiṣyate abhedaikatvasaṃkhyāyāṃ godau tatra na sidhyati  BVaky prāg vṛtter yuktavadbhāve ṣaṣṭhī bhedāśrayā bhavet vṛttau saṃkhyāviśeṣāṇāṃ tyāgād bhedo nivartate  BVaky vidyamānāsu saṃkhyāsu ke cit saṃkhyāntaraṃ viduḥ abhedākhyam upagrāhi vṛttau tac copajāyate  BVaky vyāpāraṃ yāti bhedākhyais tat svair avayavaiḥ kva cit ātmā bhedānapekṣo sya kva cid eti nimittatām  BVaky dāsyāḥ patir iti vyakto godāv iti ca dṛśyate vyāpārabhedaḥ saṃkhyāyās tasmād eva vyavasthitaḥ  BVaky dvyādināṃ ca dviputrādau bāhyo bhedo nivartate vibhaktivācyaḥ svārthatvān nimittaṃ tv avatiṣṭhate  BVaky dvitvopasarjane saṅghe dviśabdas tatra vartate so yam ity abhisaṃbandhād ubhaśabde na tat tathā  BVaky ubhayas tatra tulyārtho vṛttau nityaṃ prayujyate sūtre pi nityagrahaṇaṃ tadartham abhidhīyate  BVaky āpi ke cāparārthatvān nābheda upajāyate ubhe iti tataḥ svārthe bhede vṛttiḥ prayujyate  BVaky strītvābhidhānapakṣe pi guṇabhāvaviparyayaḥ svabhāvād aparārthatvāt tatra bhedo na hīyate  BVaky tasmād dvivacanāṭ ṭāpaś cobhayo nyatra dṛśyate pratyayaṃ tayapaṃ hitvā nāsty uttarapade punaḥ  BVaky prāptiḥ pragṛhyasaṃjñāyā na syāt pratyayalakṣaṇāt kumāryagāre na hy asti samāso vacanāntare  BVaky ekadvayor yañādināṃ vibhāṣā luṅ na kalpate yauṣmākas tāvakaś ceti bhedābhāvān na sidhyati  BVaky dṛṣṭo gārgyatare bhedas tathā gargatarā iti yuṣmatpitā tvatpiteti tathādeśau vyavasthitau  BVaky upādhibhūtā yā saṃkhyā prakṛtau samavasthitā ādeśaiḥ samjnayā vāpi vibhaktyā vyajyate vinā  BVaky śaurpike māsajāte ca parimāṇaṃ svabhāvataḥ upādhibhūtām āśritya saṃkhyāṃ bhedena vartate  BVaky vayasvini paricchedaḥ krīte cāpi na gamyate iṣṭo bhedād ṛte tatra patimāṇam anarthakam  BVaky bhinnasyābhedavacanāt prasthādibhyaḥ śaso vidhiḥ taddharmatvād abhedāt tu ghaṭādibhyo na dṛśyate  BVaky śrūyate vacanaṃ yatra bhāvas tatra viśiṣyate nivartate yad vacanaṃ tasya bhāvo na vidyate  BVaky kāryaṃ sattāśrayaṃ śāstrād apravṛttir adarśanam vākye dṛṣṭaṃ yad atyantam abhāvas tasya vṛttiṣu  BVaky samjñāviṣayabhedārthaṃ prasaktādarśanaṃ smṛtam śrūyamānaṃ tu vacanaṃ viśiṣṭam upalabhyate  BVaky abhāvo vā luko yatra rūpavān vā vidhīyate vyabhicārān nimittasya tatrāsādhuḥ prasajyate  BVaky bhedaḥ saṃkhyāviśeṣo vā vyākhyāto vṛttivākyayoḥ sarvatraiva viśeṣas tu nāvaśyaṃ tādṛśo bhavet  BVaky āteś ca bhedahetutvān na liṅgena viśeṣyate pradhānaṃ mṛgadugdhādau gārgīputre na sa kramaḥ  BVaky abhede liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ yogāc chuklaṃ paṭā iti prasakte śāstram ārabdhaṃ siddhaye liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ  BVaky parārthaṃ śeṣabhāvaṃ yo vṛttiṣu pratipadyate guṇo viśeṣaṇatvena sa sūtre vyapadiśyate  BVaky śabdāntaratvād vākyeṣu viśeṣā yady api śrutāḥ vṛtter abhinnarūpatvāt teṣu vṛttir na vidyate  BVaky rūpāc ca śabdasaṃskāraḥ sāmānyaviṣayo yataḥ tasmāt tadāśrayaṃ liṅgaṃ vacanaṃ ca prasajyate  BVaky saliṅgaṃ ca sasaṃkhyaṃ ca tato dravyābhidhāyinā saṃbadhyate padaṃ tatra tayor bhinnā śrutir bhavet  BVaky bhāvino bahiraṅgasya vacanād āśrayasya ye liṅgasaṃkhye guṇānāṃ te sūtreṇa pratipādite  BVaky viśeṣavṛtter api ca rūpābhedād alakṣitaḥ yasmād viśeṣas tenātra bhedakāryaṃ na kalpate  BVaky viśeṣa eva sāmānyaṃ viśesād bhidyate yataḥ abhedo hi viśeṣāṇām āśrito vinivartakaḥ  BVaky yad yad āśrīyate tat tad anyasya vinivartakam bhedābhedavibhāgas tu sāmānye na nirūpyate  BVaky apoddhāraś ca sāmānyam iti tasyopakārinaḥ nimittāvastham evātas tat svadharmeṇa gṛhyate  BVaky anirdhāritadharmatvād bhedā eva vikalpitāḥ nimittair vyapadiśyante sāmānyākhyāviśesitāḥ  BVaky yadā tu vyapadiśyete liṅgasaṃkhye svabhāvataḥ prayogeṣv eva sādhutvaṃ vākye prakramyate tadā  BVaky tatra prayogo niyato guṇānām āśrayaiḥ saha sāmānyaṃ yat tad atyantaṃ tatraiva samavasthitam  BVaky na gotvaṃ śābaleyasya gaur iti vyapadiśyate śuklatvaṃ bāhuleyasya śukla ity apadiśyate  BVaky vyatireke ca saty evaṃ matupaḥ śravanaṃ bhavet lug anvākhyāyate tasmād rasādibhyaś ca nāsti saḥ  BVaky yat so yam iti saṃbandhād rūpābhedena vartate śuklādivat tato lopas tad rasādau na vidyate  BVaky āveśo liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ kva cin mañcādivat sthitah so yam ity abhisaṃbandhe sa prasthādau na vidyate  BVaky liṅgam liṅgaparityāge sūtraṃ pratyayaśāsanam so yam ity abhisaṃbandhāt puṃśabde stryabhidhāyini  BVaky āśraye liṅgasaṃkhyābhyām āśritaṃ vyapadiśyate viśeṣaṇānāṃ cājāter iti śāstravyavasthayā  BVaky nimittānuvidhāyitvād ye dharmā bhedahetuṣu ta āśraye pi vidyanta iti buddhir nivartyate  BVaky ākhyāyate ca śāstreṇa lokarūḍhā svabhāvataḥ nimittatulyā godādau pravṛttir liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ  BVaky haritakyādiṣu vyaktiḥ saṃkhyā khalatikādiṣu manuṣyalubviśeṣāṇām abhidheyāśrayaṃ dvayam  BVaky jātiprayoge jātyā cet saṃbandham upagacchati viśeṣaṇaṃ tato dharmāñ jātes tat pratipadyate  BVaky lubante saṃnipatitaṃ jāter anyad viśeṣaṇam lubantasya pradhānatvāt taddharmair vyapadiśyate  BVaky nañsamāsabahuvrīhi dvandvastryatiśayeṣu ye bhedā bhāṣyānusāreṇa vācyās te liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ  BVaky yadi ṣaṣṭhīdvitīyāntān nikṛṣṭāt tamabādayaḥ nyakkāriṇi syur utkṛṣṭe prakṛteḥ syād viliṅgatā  BVaky kālyāṃ kālād dvitīyāntāt kāle kālyās tarab bhavet nyakkāriṇi tathā gārgye gargebhyaḥ pratyayo bhavet  BVaky nyakkartṛṣu ca gargeṣu gārgyāt syāt tac ca neṣyate kumāryāḥ svārthike ṅīp syāt prakṛtyartho hi nādhikaḥ  BVaky ṣaṣṭhyantād adhike tasmād guṇe svāśrayavartini utkṛṣṭasamavetāyāṃ kriyāyāṃ vā vidhīyate  BVaky upāttaṃ ca prakṛtyartho dravyam evāśrayas tayoḥ so yam ity abhisaṃbandhād abhedena pratīyate  BVaky rūpābhedāc ca tad dravyam ākāṅkṣāvat pratīyate viśeṣair bhinnarūpais tad āśrayair iva yujyate  BVaky bhinnarūpesu yal liṅgaṃ viśeṣesu vyavasthitam saṃkhyā ca tābhyām dravyātmā so bhinno vyapadiśyate  BVaky āśrayaḥ samavāyi ca nimittaṃ liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ kartṛsthabhāvakaḥ śetir ato bhāṣya udāhṛtaḥ  BVaky nimittam āśrayatvena gṛhyeta yadi sādhanam karmāpadiṣṭayoḥ prāptis tatra syāl liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ  BVaky śāstre nimittabhāvena samudāyād apoddhṛtaḥ stryarthas tasyecchayā yogaḥ prakṛtyā pratyayena vā  BVaky strīśabdo guṇaśabdatvāt tulyadharmā sitādibhiḥ guṇamātre prayujyeta saṃstyānavati vāśraye  BVaky stryarthaḥ saṃstyānavad dravyaṃ prakṛtyarthaś ca yady asau dravyopalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ saṃstyānasya tathā sati  BVaky saṃstyānena kva cid dravyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yady upalakṣitam anaṅgīkṛtasaṃstyānāt tadvṛtteḥ pratyayo bhavet  BVaky bhūtādayaḥ ṣaḍākhyāś ca saṃstyānenopalakṣite brāhmaṇyādau yadā vṛttās tebhyaḥ syuḥ pratyayās tadā  BVaky tadvanto hi pradhānatvāt pratyayāṇām prayojakāḥ sāmānādhikaraiṇye pi tasmāṭ ṭābādisaṃbhavaḥ  BVaky guṇamātrābhidhāyitvaṃ strīśabde varṇyate yadā prakṛtyarthaś ca saṃstyānaṃ svārthikāḥ pratyayās tadā  BVaky saṃstyāne kevale vṛttiḥ prakṛtīnām na vidyate tadāviṣṭe tato dravye gṛhyante samavasthitāḥ  BVaky upakāri ca saṃstyānaṃ yeṣu śabdeṣv apekṣitam tebhyaṣ ṭābādayas tac ca bhūtādiṣv avivakṣitam  BVaky saṃstyānaṃ pratyayasyārthaḥ śuddham āśrīyate yadā tadā dvivacanāneka pratyayatvaṃ na sidhyati  BVaky jātiś cet strītvam evāsau bhedo nyatrāvivakṣitaḥ yasmād bhinnair api dravyais tad ekaṃ sad viśiṣyate  BVaky mātrāṇām hi tirobhāve parimāṇam na vidyate kumārya iti tena syāt kumāryāṃ bhedasaṃbhavāt  BVaky jātisaṃkhyāsamāhārair yathaiva sahacāriṇi dravye kriyāḥ pravartanta ekātmatve vyapekṣite  BVaky mūrtibhyo mūrtidharmāṇām tathābhedasya darśanāt sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca kriyāyogaś ca kalpate  BVaky sāmānādhikaraṇye tu matublopād apekṣite luk taddhitalukīti syāl luk tatrāpy upalakṣaṇam  BVaky kesāṃ cit tyaktabhedeṣu dravyeṣv eva vidhīyate saṃstyānavatsu ṭābādir abhedena samanvayāt  BVaky sāmānyabhūto dravyātmā paricchinnaparigrahaḥ kriyābhir yujyate bhedair bhāgaśaś cāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky śuklādiṣv āśrayadravyaṃ prādhānyenābhidhīyate strītvaṃ tu pratyayārthatvād abhidhāviṣayo yataḥ  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhād āśrayaṃ pratipadyate strītvaṃ svabhāvasiddho vā guṇabhāvaviparyayaḥ  BVaky sākāṅkṣatvād guṇatvena sāmānyaṃ vopadiśyate vyaktīnām ātmadharmo sāv ekaprakhyānibandhanaḥ  BVaky evambhūtā ca sāvasthā bhāgabhedaparigrahe kṛte buddhyaiva bhedānām āśrayatve ca kalpite  BVaky niskṛṣṭeṣv api bhedeṣu vyaktirūpāśraye tataḥ liṅgapratyavamarśena liṅgasaṃkhye prapadyate  BVaky antarena caśabdasya prayogaṃ dvandvabhāvinām aviśiṣṭārthavṛttitvaṃ rūpābhedāt pratīyate  BVaky vikalpavati vā vṛttir nivartye tha samuccite teṣām ajñātaśaktīnāṃ dyotakena niyamyate  BVaky vṛttau viśiṣṭarūpatvāc caśabdo vinivartate arthabhede pi sārūpyāt tac cārthenāpadiśyate  BVaky casya cāsattvabhūto rthaḥ sa evāśriyate yadi taddharmatvaṃ tato dvandve cādiṣv arthakṛtaṃ hi tat  BVaky cārthaḥ śabde kva cid bhedāt kathaṃ cit samavasthitaḥ dyotakāś cādayas tasya vaktā dvandvas tu tadvatām  BVaky vikalpādyabhidheyasya cārthasyānyapadārthatā dyotakatvān na kalpeta tasmāt sad upalakṣyate  BVaky tatra svābhāvikaṃ liṅgaṃ śabdadharme vyapekṣite śabdaḥ kaś cit tam evārthaṃ kathaṃ cit pratipadyate  BVaky śabdād arthāḥ pratāyante sa bhedānāṃ vidhāyakaḥ anumānaṃ vivakṣāyāḥ śabdād anyan na vidyate  BVaky samuccitaḥ syād dvandvārtho guṇabhūtasamuccayaḥ samuccayo vāpi bhaved guṇabhūtasamuccitaḥ  BVaky samuccitasya prādhānye liṅgasaṃkhye svabhāvataḥ samuccayasya prādhānye śāstraṃ syāt pratipādakam  BVaky samuccayavato rthasya prādhānye py apare viduḥ nimittānuvidhāyitvād asiddhim liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ  BVaky samuccayo nimittaṃ cet syān nimittānuvartanam anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ cārtho dvandvanibandhanaḥ  BVaky samuccitanimittatve cārthasyāpagame pi vā svabhāvasiddhe dvandvasya liṅgasaṃkhye vyavasthite  BVaky padāntarasthasyārthasya dyotakatvān na yujyate nipāto liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ dvandvas tv arthasya vācakaḥ  BVaky nimittānuvidhāne ca dravyadharmānapekṣaṇāt guṇapradhānabhāvena kriyāyogo na kalpate  BVaky yasya nāsti kriyāyogaḥ svatantro sau na vidyate artho dvandvasya tatra syād upādānam anarthakam  BVaky samuccayavato rthasya vācako nānuvartate nimittam api cāsyārthaḥ svadharmair yujyate tataḥ  BVaky bāhyo nāsty āśrayo dvandve viśeṣau tatra hi śrutau samuccayas tadādhāras taddharmair vyapadiśyate  BVaky yo vāvayavabhedābhyāṃ bhedavadbhyām ivānvitaḥ ekaḥ samūho dharmān sa bhāgayoḥ pratipadyate  BVaky ekaś ca dvyātmako rtho sau bhedābhedasamanvitaḥ yau bhedāv āśritas tatsthe liṅgasaṃkhye prapadyate  BVaky yathā svaśabdābhihite caitrārthe na prayujyate caitraśabdo bahuvrihāv aprayogas tathā bhavet  BVaky yathā gaur iti śuklāder abhidhānaṃ na vidyate evaṃ yasyābhisaṃbandho gobhis tāvat pratīyate  BVaky saṃbandhī niyato rūḍhaś citrāṇāṃ na ca vidyate gavāṃ yathā vajrapāṇis tryakṣe vā pi vyavasthitaḥ  BVaky śabdāntaratvād vākyeṣu viśeṣā yady api śrutāḥ vṛttiśabdo nya evāyaṃ sāmānyasyābhidhāyakaḥ  BVaky agor acitragoś caiva rūpabhedān nivartakaḥ na citragur viśeṣāṇāṃ rūpābhedāt tu vācakaḥ  BVaky yathā citragur ity etat prayukte na prayujyate evaṃ yadi syāt sāmānyaṃ tasya na syāt pratiśrutiḥ  BVaky sarvādayo viśeṣās tu pradeśānāṃ nivartakāḥ yathā pradeśāḥ sāmānya pradeśāntarabādhakāḥ  BVaky vibhaktyarthābhidhānād vā ṣaṣṭhī nānuprayujyate dravyasyānabhidhānāt tu tacchabdo nuprayujyate  BVaky sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ cen matublopāt prakalpate matupo pi tadarthatvād anavasthā prasajyate  BVaky saṃbandhasya ca saṃbandī saṃbandho nyaḥ prasajyate vibhaktyarthapradhāne ca kriyāyogo na kalpate  BVaky vibhaktyarthapradhānatvāt tatas tatreti na kriyā dṛśyādiḥ karmakartrādi nimittatvāya kalpate  BVaky antarbhavec ca saṃbandhaḥ prādhānyābhihitaḥ katham sa prātipadikārthaś ca tathābhūtaḥ kathaṃ bhatvet  BVaky asaṃbhavāt tu saṃbandhe saṃbandhasahacāriṇi jātisaṃkhyāsamāhāra kāryāṇām iva saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhād viśiṣṭāśrayavācinām śuklādival liṅgasaṃkhye śāstrārambhād bhaviṣyataḥ  BVaky bhedena tu vivakṣāyāṃ sāmānye vā vivakṣite saliṅgasya sasaṃkhyasya padārthasyāgatir bhavet  BVaky sādhutvaṃ na vibhaktyartha mātre vṛttasya dṛśyate kṛtsnārthavṛtteḥ sādhutvam ity arthagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhād dravyavṛttir ayaṃ yadā saliṅgasya sasaṃkhyasya tadā sādhutvam ucyate  BVaky antarbhūtavibhaktyarthe ṣaṣṭhī na śrūyate yathā tathāśrutiḥ prasajyeta liṅgasaṃkhyābhidhāyinām  BVaky sādharmyam avyayena syād bahuvrīhes tathā sati liṅgasaṃkhyānimittasya saṃskārasyāpavartanāt  BVaky prayuktena ca saṃbandhāc caitrādiśravanaṃ bhavet vinā vibhaktyā saṃbandho vibhaktyā vidyate vinā  BVaky abhidhāne pi saṃkhyāyāḥ saṃkhyātvaṃ na nivartate ṣaṣṭhyarthasyābhidhāne tu syāt prātipadikārthatā  BVaky anuprayogasiddhyarthaṃ na vibhaktyarthakalpanā vastvantaram upakṣiptam iti ke cit pracakṣate  BVaky saṃbandibhir viśiṣṭānām saṃbandhānāṃ nimittatā saṃbandhair vā viśiṣṭānāṃ tadvatāṃ syān nimittatā  BVaky ke cit saṃyogino daṇḍād viṣāṇāt samavāyinaḥ tadvati pratyayān āhur bahuvrīhiṃ tathaiva ca  BVaky bhinnaṃ saṃbandhibhedena saṃbandham apare viduḥ nimittaṃ sa vibhaktyarthaḥ samāsenābhidhīyate  BVaky pradhānam anyārthatayā bhinnaṃ svair upasarjanaiḥ nimittam abbidheyaṃ vā sarvapaścād apekṣyate  BVaky svāmini vyatirekaś ca vākye yady api dṛśyate prādhānya eva tasyeṣṭo bahuvrīhir vivakṣite  BVaky gavāṃ viśeṣaṇatvena yadā tadvān pravartate asyaitā iti tatrārthe bahuvrīhir na vidyate  BVaky yadā pratyavamarśas tu tāsāṃ svāmī gavām iti gobhis tadābhisaṃbandho nimittatvāya kalpate  BVaky apekṣamānaḥ saṃbandhaṃ rūḍhitvasya nivṛttaye nimittānuvidhāyitvāt taddharmārthaḥ prasajyate  BVaky nānā citrā iti yathā nimittam anurudhyate nānābhūte pi vṛttaḥ san bahuvrīhis tathā bhavet  BVaky saṃbandhini nimitte tu dravyadharmo na hīyate liṅgābhāvo hi liṅgasya virodhitvena vartate  BVaky saṃkhvāvāṃl liṅgavāmś cārtho bhinnadharmānimittataḥ āsanna eva dravyatvāt taddharmair na virudhyate  BVaky vibhaktyarthena cāviṣṭaṃ śuddhaṃ ceti dvidhā sthitam dravyaṃ śuddhasya yo dharmaḥ sa na syād anyadharmaṇaḥ  BVaky dravyamātrasya nirdeśe bhedo yam avivakṣitaḥ granthe pūrvatra bhedas tu dvitīye nupradarśitaḥ  BVaky dravyasya grahaṇaṃ cātra liṅgasaṃkhyāviśeṣaṇam dravyāśritatvaṃ hi tayos tato nyasya na sidhyataḥ  BVaky saṃbandhibhinnasaṃbandha parichinne pravartate samāso dravyasāmānye viśiṣṭārthānupātini  BVaky dravyadharmānatikrānto bhedadharmeṣv avasthitaḥ bhaviṣyadāśrayāpekṣe liṅgasaṃkhye prapadyate  BVaky śāstrapravṛttibhede pi laukiko rtho na bhidyate nañsamase yatas tatra trayaḥ pakṣā vicāritāḥ  BVaky śabdāntare pi caikatvam āśrityaivaṃ vicāraṇā abrahmaṇādiṣu nañaḥ prayogo na hi vidyate  BVaky prāk samāsāt padārthānāṃ nivṛttir dyotyate nañā svabhāvato nivṛttānāṃ rūpābhedād alakṣitā  BVaky brāhmaṇādisthayā vākyeṣv ākhyātapadavācyayā kriyayā yasya saṃbandho vṛttis tasya na vidyate  BVaky pācakādipadasthā cen nañā saṃbadhyate kriyā tatra sattānupādānāt tripakṣī nopapadyate  BVaky sattayaivābhisaṃbandho yadi sarvatra kalpyate asann iti samāse smin sattānyā parikalpyatām  BVaky ktvānte ca tumunante ca nañsamāse na dṛśyate viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ nañāsattābhidhāyinā  BVaky kriyāyāḥ sādhanādhāra sāmānye nañ vyavasthitaḥ tato viśiṣṭair ādhārair yujyate brāhmaṇādibhiḥ  BVaky vṛttau yathā gatādyartham upādāya nirādayaḥ yujyante sādhanādhārair nañsamāse pi sa kramaḥ  BVaky tatrāsati naño vṛtter brāhmaṇakṣatriyādibhiḥ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ kalpyate kubjakhañjavat  BVaky kāmacāre ca saty evam asataḥ syāt pradhānatā guṇatvam itareṣāṃ ca teṣāṃ vā syāt pradhānatā  BVaky prādhānyenāśritāḥ pūrvaṃ śruteḥ sāmānyavṛttayaḥ viśeṣa eva prakrāntā brāhmaṇakṣatrivādavaḥ  BVaky yathā gaurādibhis teṣām avacchedo vidhīyate asatāpy anabhivyaktaṃ tādātmyaṃ vyajyate tathā  BVaky yathā sattābhidhānāya sann arthaḥ parikalpyate tathāsattābhidhānāya nirupākhyo pi kalpate  BVaky kṣatriyādau padaṃ kṛtvā buddhiḥ sattāntarāśrayā jātyā bhinnāṃ tataḥ sattāṃ prasaktām apakarṣati  BVaky abhāva iti bhāvasya pratiṣedhe vivakṣite sopākhyatvam anāśritya pratiṣedho na kalpate  BVaky anekadharmavacanāḥ śabdāḥ saṅghābhidhāyinaḥ ekadeśeṣu vartante tulyarūpāḥ svabhāvataḥ  BVaky yathaikadeśakaraṇāt kṛta itv abhidhīyate akṛtaś ceti saṃghātaḥ sa evābrāhmaṇe kramaḥ  BVaky brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇas tasmād upanyāsāt prasajyate akṛte vā kṛtāsaṅgād aviśiṣṭaṃ kṛtākṛtāt  BVaky amukhyasaṃbhave tatra mukhyasya vinivṛttaye śāstrānvākhyānasamaye nañ prayukto viśeṣakaḥ  BVaky padārthānupaghātena dṛśyate nyaviśeṣaṇam atha jātimato rthasya kaś cid dharmo nivartitaḥ  BVaky avaśyaṃ brāhmaṇe kaś cit kva cid dharmo na vidyate viśeṣāvacanāt tatra nañaḥ śrutir anarthikā  BVaky aviśiṣṭasya paryāyo nañviśiṣṭaḥ prasajyate anvākhyānād dhi sādhutvam evaṃbhūte pratīyate  BVaky padārthānupaghātena yady apy atra viśeṣaṇam upacārasato rthasya sāvasthā dyotyate nañā  BVaky viśeṣyeṣu yathābhūtaḥ padārthaḥ samavasthitaḥ tathābhūte tathābhāvo gamyate bhedahetubhiḥ  BVaky nivṛtte vayavas tasmin padārthe vartate katham nānimittā hi śabdasya pravṛttir upapadyate  BVaky ārāc chabdavad ekasya viruddhe rthe svabhāvataḥ śabdasya vṛttir yady asti nañaḥ śrutir anarthikā  BVaky atha svabhāvo vacanād anvākhyeyatvam arhati tad vācyam aprasiddhatvān nañārtho vinivartyate  BVaky yady apy ubhayavṛttitvaṃ pradhānaṃ tu pratīyate prasthānaṃ gamyate śuddhe tadarthe pi na tiṣṭhatau  BVaky kimartham atathābhūte sati mukhyārthasaṃbhave bhede brāhmaṇaśabdasya vṛttir abhyupagamyate  BVaky ayaṃ padārtha etasmin kṣatriyādau na vidyate iti tadvacanaḥ śabdaḥ pratyayāya prayujyate  BVaky buddher viṣayatāṃ prāpte śabdād arthe pratīyate pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā grutyā hy artho nusajyate  BVaky asamyagupadeśād vā nimittāt saṃśayasya vā śabdapravṛttir na tv asti loṣṭādiṣu viparyayāt  BVaky anekasmād asa iti prādhānye sati sidhyati sāpekṣatvaṃ pradhānānām evaṃ yuktaṃ tvatalvidhau  BVaky ekasya ca pradhānatvāt tadviśeṣaṇasaṃnidhau pradhānadharmāvyāvṛttir ato na vacanāntaram  BVaky
