pradhānam atra bhedyatvād ekārtho vikṛto nañā hitvā svadharmān vartante dvyādayo py ekatāṃ gatāḥ  BVaky brāhmaṇatvaṃ yathāpannā nañyuktāḥ kṣatriyādayaḥ dvitvādiṣu tathaikatvaṃ nañyogād upacaryate  BVaky ekatvayogam āsādya sa dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate dvyādibhyas teṣu tacchabdo vartate brāhmaṇādivat  BVaky āviṣṭasaṃkhyo vākye sau yathā dvyādau prayujyate vṛttau tasya pradhānatvāt sā saṃkhyā na nivartate  BVaky pratiṣedhyo yathābhūtas tathābhūto nuṣajyate vacanāntarayoge hi na so rthaḥ pratiṣidhyate  BVaky aśukla iti kṛṣṇādir yathārthaḥ saṃpratīyate saṃkhyāntaraṃ tathāneka ity atrāpy abhidhīyate  BVaky kriyāprasaṅgāt sarveṣu karmasv aṅgīkṛteṣu ca ekasmin pratiṣiddhe pi prāptam anyat pratīyate  BVaky kriyāśrutiś ca prakrānte prasajyapratiṣedhane paryudāse tu niyataṃ saṃkhyeyāntaram ucyate  BVaky dhātvarthaḥ karmaviṣayo vyapadiṣṭaḥ svasādhanaiḥ arthāt sarvāṇi karmāṇi prāg ākṣipyāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky nirjñātasādhanādhāre yatrākhyāte prayujyate aneka iti paścāc ca tiṣṭhatīty anuṣajyate  BVaky sādhyatvāt tatra siddhena kriyā dravyeṇa lakṣyate prāg evāṅgīkṛtaṃ dravyam ataḥ pūrveṇa bhidyate  BVaky saṃkhyaiva pratiṣedhena saṃkhyāntaram apekṣate vākye pi tena naikatva mātram eva nivartyate  BVaky snehāntarād avacchedas tathāsatteḥ pratīyate tailena bhojane prāpte na tv anyad upasecanam  BVaky ekārthe vartamānābhyām asatā brāhmaṇena ca yadā jātyantaraṃ bāhyaṃ kṣatriyādy apadiśyate  BVaky śyāmeva śastrī kanyeti yathānyad vyapadiśyate asan brāhmaṇa ity ābhyāṃ tathānye kṣatriyādayaḥ  BVaky asāsno gaur iti yathāgavayo vyapadiśyate jātyantaraṃ na gor eva sasnābhāvaḥ pratīyate  BVaky tulyarūpaṃ yathākhyātaṃ kaṇṭakair bhedahetubhiḥ khadiraṃ jātibhedena kharjūrāt pratipadyate  BVaky avidyamānabrāhmaṇyo yādṛśo brāhmaṇo bhavet aṅgīkṛtopamānena tathānyo rtho bhidhīyate  BVaky avṛṣṭayo yathā varsā nīhārābhrasamāvṛtāḥ tadrūpatvāt sa hemanta ity abhinnaḥ pratīyate  BVaky apare brāhmaṇādīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ jātivācinām dravyasyānyapadārthatve nañā yogaṃ pracakṣate  BVaky na caivaṃviṣayaḥ kaś cid bahuvrīhiḥ prakalpate agur aśva iti vyāptir nañsamāsena yasya na  BVaky dvandvaikadeśinor uktā paravalliṅgatā yataḥ avarṣāsu tato siddhir iṣṭayor liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ  BVaky viśeṣaṇaṃ brāhmaṇādi kriyāsaṃbandhino sataḥ yadā viṣayabhinnaṃ tat tadāsattvam pratīyate  BVaky brāhmaṇatvena cāsattvād ucyate sat tad anyathā asad ity api sattvena sataḥ sattā nivartyate  BVaky samanyadravyavṛttitvān nimittānuvidhāyinaḥ ayogo liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ syād vā sāmānyadharmatā  BVaky prāg asattvābhidhāyitvaṃ samāse dravyavācitā nimittānuvidhānaṃ ca na sarvatra svabhāvataḥ  BVaky nimittānuvidhāne ca kriyāyogo na kalpate tathā cāvyapadeśyatvād upādānam anarthakam  BVaky asatsāmānyavṛttir vā viśeṣaiḥ kṣatriyādibhiḥ prayuktair āśrayair bhinno yāti talliṅgasaṃkhyatām  BVaky prāg āśrayo hi bhedāya pradhāne bhyantarīkṛtaḥ punaḥ pratyavamarśena vibhakta iva dṛśyate  BVaky samāse śrūyate svārtho yena tadvāṃs tadāśrayaḥ dravyaṃ tu liṅgasaṃkhyāvad asatābhyantarīkṛtam  BVaky ekārthaviṣayau śabdau tasminn anyārthavartinau asataiva tu bhedānāṃ sarveṣām upasaṃgrahaḥ  BVaky te kṣatriyādibhir vācyā vācyā vā sarvanāmabhiḥ yāntīvānyapadārthatvaṃ naño rūpāvikalpanāt  BVaky viśeṣasyāprayoge tu liṅgasaṃkhye na sidhyataḥ avarṣādiṣu dosaś ca hemanto nyāśrayo yataḥ  BVaky ākṛtiḥ sarvaśabdānāṃ yadā vācyā pratīyate ekatvād ekaśabdatvaṃ nyāyyaṃ tasyāś ca varṇyate  BVaky āviṣṭaliṅgatā tasyāṃ syād grāmyapagusaṅghavat dravyabhede pi caikatvāt tatraikavacanaṃ bhavet  BVaky āśrayāṇāṃ hi liṅgaiḥ sā niyatair eva yujyate tathā ca yuktavadbhāve pratiṣedho nirarthakaḥ  BVaky sarvatrāviṣṭaliṅgatvaṃ lokaliṅgaparigrahe virodhitvāt prasajyeta nāśritaṃ tac ca laukikam  BVaky sāmānyam ākṛtir bhāvo jātir ity atra laukikam liṅgaṃ na saṃbhavaty eva tenānyat parigṛhyate  BVaky pravṛttir iti sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tasya kathyate āvirbhāvas tirobhāvaḥ sthitiś cety atha bhidyate  BVaky pravṛttimantaḥ sarve rthās tisṛbhiś ca pravṛttibhiḥ satataṃ na viyujyante vācaś caivātra saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky yaś cāpravṛttidharmārthaś citirūpeṇa gṛhyate anuyātīva so nyeṣāṃ pravṛttīr viśvagāśrayāḥ  BVaky tenāsya citirūpaṃ ca citikālaś ca bhidyate tasya svarūpabhedas tu na kaś cid api vidyate  BVaky acetaneṣu caitanyaṃ saṃkrāntam iva dṛśyate pratibimbakadharmeṇa yat tac chabdanibandhanam  BVaky avasthā tādṛśī nāsti yā liṅgena na yujyate kva cit tu śabdasaṃskāro liṅgasyānāśraye sati  BVaky kṛttaddhitābhidheyānāṃ bhāvānāṃ na virudhyate śāstre liṅgaṃ guṇāvasthā tathā cākṛtir iṣyate  BVaky liṅgaṃ prati na bhedo sti dravyapakṣe pi kaś cana tasmāt sapta vikalpā ye saivātrāviṣṭaliṅgatā  BVaky vacane niyamaḥ śāstrād dravyasyābhyupagamyate yatas tad ākṛtau śāstram anyathaiva samarthyate  BVaky vartate yo bahuṣv artho bhede tasya vivakṣite svāśrayair vyapadiṣṭasya śāstre vacanam ucyate  BVaky yadā tv āśrayabhedena bheda eva pratīyate ākṛter dravyapakṣena tadā bhedo na vidyate  BVaky abhede tv ekaśabdatvāc chāstrāc ca vacane sati ekaśeṣo na vaktavyo vacanānāṃ ca saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky nanu cānabhidheyatve dravyasya tadapāśrayaḥ ākṛter upakāro yaṃ dravyābhāvān na kalpate  BVaky vyapadeśo bhidheyena na śāstre kaś cid āśritaḥ dravyaṃ nāma padārtho yo na ca sa pratiṣidhyate  BVaky guṇabhāvo bhidheyatvaṃ prati dravyasya nāśritaḥ upakāri guṇaḥ śeṣaḥ parārtha iti kalpanā  BVaky dravye na guṇabhāvo sti vinādravyābhidhāyitām ākṛtau vā pradhānatvam ata evaṃ samarthyate  BVaky kaiś cid guṇapradhānatvaṃ nāmākhyātavad iṣyate na vṛttivat parārthasya guṇabhāvas tu varṇyate  BVaky guṇabhūtasya nānātvād ākṛter ekaśabdatā siddho vacanabhedaś ca dravyabhedasamanvayāt  BVaky sādhanaṃ guṇabhāvena kriyāyā bhedakaṃ yathā ākhyāteṣv ekaśabdāyā jāter dravyaṃ tathocyate  BVaky ekatve tulyarūpatvāc chabdānāṃ pratipādane nimittāt tadvato rthasya viśiṣṭagrahaṇe sati  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhād āśrayair ākṛteḥ saha pravṛttau bhinnaśabdāyāṃ liṅgasaṃkhye prasidhyataḥ  BVaky prāk ca jātyabhisaṃbandhāt sarvanāmābhidheyatā vastūpalakṣaṇaṃ sattve prayujyante tyadādayaḥ  BVaky pākau pākā iti yathā bhedakaḥ kaiś cid āśrayaḥ iṣyate cānupādāno dharmo sau guṇavācinām  BVaky āśrayasyānupādāne kevalaṃ labhate yadi ādhāradharmān sāmānyaṃ purastāt tad vicāritam  BVaky jātau pūrvaṃ pravṛttānāṃ śabdānāṃ jātivācinām aśabdavācyāt saṃbandhād vyaktir apy upajāyate  BVaky so yam ity abhisaṃbandhāj jātidharmopacaryate dravyaṃ tadāśrayo bhedo jāteś cābhyupagamyate  BVaky mañcaśabdo yathādheyaṃ mañceṣv eva vyavasthitaḥ tattvenāha tathā jāti śabdo dravyeṣu vartate  BVaky tatra jātipadārthatvaṃ tathaivābhyupagamyate jātir utsṛṣṭasaṃkhyā tu dravyātmany anuṣajyate  BVaky asyedam iti vā yatra so yam ity api vā śrutiḥ vartate paradharmeṇa tad anyad abhidhīyate  BVaky yat pradhānaṃ na tasyāsti svarūpam anirūpanāt guṇasya cātmanā dravyaṃ tadbhāvenopalakṣyate  BVaky guṇasya bhedakāle tu prādhānyam upajāyate saṃsargaśrutir artheṣu sākṣād eva na vartate  BVaky jātau vṛtto yadā dravye sa śabdo vartate punaḥ jāter eva padārthatvaṃ na tadābhyupagamyate  BVaky pravṛttānāṃ punar vṛttir ekatvenopavarṇyate pratipatter upāyeṣu na tattvam anugamyate  BVaky apṛthakśabdavācyasya jātir āśrīyate yadā dravyasya sati saṃsparśe tadā jātipadārthatā  BVaky dravyasya sati saṃsparśe dravyam āśrīyate yadā vācyaṃ tenaiva śabdena tadā dravyapadārthatā  BVaky apṛthakśabdavācyāpi bhedamātre pravartate yadā saṃbandhavaj jātiḥ sāpi dravyapadārthatā  BVaky atyantabhinnayor eva jātidravyābhidhāyinoḥ avācyasyopakāritva āśrite tūbhayārthatā  BVaky āśrite tv āśrayakṛtaṃ bhedam abhyupagacchatā punaś cāpy ekaśabdatvaṃ jātiśabde nuvarṇitam  BVaky anirjātasya nirjñānaṃ yena tan mānam ucyate prasthādi tena meyātmā sākalyenāvadhāryate  BVaky anirjñātaṃ prasiddhena yena taddharma gamyate sākalyenāparijñānād upamānaṃ tad ucyate  BVaky dvayoḥ samānayor dharma upamānopameyayoḥ samāsa upamānānāṃ śabdais tadabhidhāyibhiḥ  BVaky ādhārabhedād bhedo yaḥ śyāmatve so vivakṣitaḥ guṇo sāv āśritaikatvo bhinnādhāraḥ pratīyate  BVaky guṇayor niyato bhedo guṇajātes tathaikatā ekatve tyantabhede vānopamānasya saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky jātimātravyapekṣāyām upamārtho na kaś cana śyāmatvam ekaṃ guṇayor ubhayor api vartate  BVaky yenaiva hetunā śyāmā śastrī tatra pratīyate sa hetur devadattāyāḥ pratyaye na viśiṣyate  BVaky āśrayād yo guṇe bhedo jāter yā cāviśiṣṭatā tābhyām ubhābhyāṃ dravyātmā savyāpāraḥ pratīyate  BVaky so yam ekatvanānātve vyavahāraḥ samāśritaḥ bhedābhedavimarśena vyatikīrṇena vartate  BVaky śyāmety evābhidhiyeta jātimātre vivakṣite śastryādinām upādāne tatra nāsti prayojanam  BVaky aśabdavācyo yo bhedaḥ śyāmamātre na vartate śyāmeṣu keṣu cid vṛttir yasya so tra vyapekṣyate  BVaky śyāmeṣu keṣu cit kiṃ cit kiṃ cit sarvatra vartate sāmānyaṃ kaś cid ekasmiñ chyāme bhedo vyavasthitaḥ  BVaky tathā hi sati saurabhye bhedo jātyutpalādiṣu gandhānāṃ sati bhede tu sādṛśyam upalabhyate  BVaky guṇānām āśrayād bhedaḥ svato vāpy anugamyate anirdeśyād viśeṣād vā saṃkarād vā guṇāntaraiḥ  BVaky upamānaṃ prasiddhatvāt sarvatra vyatiricyate upameyatvam ādhikye sāmye vā na nivartate  BVaky anyais tu mānaṃ jātyādi bhedyasyārthasya varṇyate anirjñātasvarūpo hi jñeyo rthas tena mīyate  BVaky mitas tu svena mānena prasiddho yo guṇāśrayaḥ āśrayāntaramānāya svadharmeṇa pravartate  BVaky rūpāntareṇa saṃsparśo rūpāntaravatāṃ satām bhinnena yasya bhedyānām upamānaṃ tad ucyate  BVaky dharmaḥ samānaḥ śyāmādir upamānopameyayoḥ āśriyamānaprādhānyo dharmeṇānyena bhidyate  BVaky śastrīkumāryoḥ sadṛśaḥ śyāma ity evam āśrite vyapadeśyam aneneti nimittaṃ guṇayoḥ sthitam  BVaky yadā nimittais tadvanto gacchantīva tadātmatām bhedāśrayaṃ tadākhyānam upamānopameyayoḥ  BVaky tattvāsaṅgavivakṣāyāṃ yeṣu bhedo nivartate luptopamāni tāny āhus taddharmeṇa samāśrayāt  BVaky śastryāṃ prasiddhaṃ śyāmatvaṃ mānaṃ sā tena mīyate anyā śyāmā tu tadrūpā tenātyantaṃ na mīyate  BVaky śastriṃ svena guṇenāto mimānām āśrayāntaram asamāptaguṇaṃ siddher upamānaṃ pracakṣate  BVaky upameye sthito dharmaḥ śruto nyatrānumīyate śruto tha vopamānastha upameye numiyate  BVaky adhīyate brāhmaṇavat kṣatriyā iti dṛśyate upameyasya bhinnatvād vacanaṃ kṣatriyāśrayam  BVaky sādhāraṇaṃ bruvan dharma kva cid eva vyavasthitam sāmānyavacanaḥ śabda iti sūtre padiśyate  BVaky nābhedena na bhedena guṇo dviṣṭho bhidhīyate bhinnayor dharmayor ekaḥ śrūyate nyaḥ pratīyate  BVaky nātyantāya mimīte yat sāmānye samavasthitam sādṛśyād upameyārtha samīpe parikalpyate  BVaky mānaṃ prati samīpaṃ vā sādṛśyena pratīyate paricchedād dhi sādṛśyam iha mānopamānayoḥ  BVaky ekajātivyapekṣāyāṃ tad evety avasīyate bhedasyaiva vyapekṣāyām anyad eveti gamyate  BVaky karmatvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca bhedenaivāśritaṃ yataḥ atyantaikatvaviṣayo na syāt tenātra samśayaḥ  BVaky bhede pi tulyarūpatvāc chālīmṃ tān iti dṛśyate jātyabhedāt sa evāyam iti bhinno bhidhīyate  BVaky kathaṃ hy avayavo nyasya syād anya iti cocyate atyantabhede nānātvaṃ yatra tattvaṃ na vidyate  BVaky abhedasya vivakṣāyām ekatvaṃ saṅghasaṅghinoḥ saṅghinor na tv abhedo sti tathānyatvam udāhṛtam  BVaky tatrābhinnavyapekṣāyām upamārtho na vidyate yo hi gaur iti vijñāne hetuḥ so sti gavāntare  BVaky vyāvṛttānāṃ viśeṣāṇāṃ vyāpāre tu vivakṣite na kaś cid upakāro sti buddher buddhyantaraṃ prati  BVaky kiṃ cid yatrāsti sāmānyaṃ yadi bhedāś ca ke cana gotvaṃ goṣv asti sāmānyaṃ bhedāś ca śabalādayaḥ  BVaky sāmānyaṃ śyāmatānyaiva tad dhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ tad eva siddhyasiddhibhyāṃ bheda ity apadiśyate  BVaky śyāmatvam eva sāmānyam anyeṣām ubhayoḥ sthitam saṃpūrnatvāt tad anyasmād viśeṣa iti gamyate  BVaky ākṛtau vāpi sāmānye kva cid eva vyavasthitāḥ śyāmādau ye vasīyante viśeṣās ta ihāśritāḥ  BVaky jāter abhede bhede vā sādṛśyaṃ tat pracakṣate kaś cit kadā cit arthātmā tathābhūto padiśyate  BVaky yatrārthe pratyayābhedo na kadā cid vikalpate avidyamānabhedatvāt sa eka iti gamyate  BVaky yo rtha āśritanānātvaḥ sa evety apadiśyate vyāpāraṃ jātibhāgasya tatrāpi pratijānate  BVaky jātibhāgāśrayā prakhyā tatrābhinnā pravartate vyaktibhāgāśrayā buddhis tatra bhedena jāyate  BVaky anyatra vartamānaṃ sad bhedābhedasamanvitam nimittaṃ punar anyatra nānātveneva gṛhyate  BVaky ādhāreṣu padanyāsaṃ kṛtvopaiti tadāśrayam sa sādṛśyasya viṣaya ity anyair apadiśyate  BVaky parāpekṣe yathā bhāve kāraṇākhyā pravartate tathānyādhigamāpekṣam upamānaṃ pracakṣate  BVaky gurugiśyapitāputra kriyākālādayo yathā vyavahārās tathaupamyam apy apekṣānibandhanam  BVaky śyāmatvam upamāne ced vṛttaṃ vṛttau prayujyate upameyaṃ samāsena bāhyaṃ tatrābhidhīyate  BVaky ṭābanta eva caitrādau śyāmāśabdas tathā bhavet sūtre ca prathamābhāvān na śyāmādyupasarjanam  BVaky atha tv ekavibhaktitvād guṇatvād vopasarjanam naivaṃ tittirikalmāṣyām iṣṭaḥ strīpratyayo bhavet  BVaky satiśiṣṭabalīyastvād bāhye ṅiṣi ca saty api upamānasvaro na syāt tasmāt stryantaḥ samasyate  BVaky guṇe na copamānasthe sāpekṣatvaṃ prakalpate pradhānasya tathā na syād vyāghrādau liṅgadarśanam  BVaky tasmāt sati guṇatve pi prādhānyaṃ vigrahāntare naivaṃjātīyakaṃ śāstre saṃbhavaty upasarjanam  BVaky upameyātmani śyāmo vartamāno bhidhīyate upamāneṣv anirdiṣṭaḥ sāmarthyāt sa pratīyate  BVaky dravyamātre pi nirdiṣṭe candravaktre nugamyate viśiṣṭa eva candrastho guṇo nopaplavādayaḥ  BVaky bhedabhāvanayaitac ca samāse py upavarṇyate viśiṣṭaguṇabhinne rthe padam anyat prayujyate  BVaky yadi bhinnādhikaraṇo vacanād anugamyate mṛgīva capalety atra puṃvadbhāvo na sidhyati  BVaky astrīpūrvapadatvāt tu puṃvadbhāvo bhaviṣyati yathaiva mṛgadugdhādau na cet stryartho vivakṣyate  BVaky śastrīva śastrīśyāmeti devadattaiva kathyate tasyām evobhayaṃ tasmād ucyate śāstravigrahe  BVaky puṃvadbhāvasya siddhyarthaṃ pakṣe strīpratyayasya ca bahv apekṣyam atas tasyām ubhayapratipādanam  BVaky śyāmā śastrī yathā śyāmā śastrīkalpeti cocyate tatropamānetarayoḥ śyāmety etad apekṣyate  BVaky atha śyāmeva śastrīyaṃ śyāmety evaṃ prayujyate śastrī yatheyam śyāmeti tāvad eva pratīyate  BVaky upalakṣaṇamātrārthā guṇasyāsya yadi śrutiḥ pṛthag dvayoḥ śruto py eṣa neṣṭasvārthasya vācakaḥ  BVaky upameyaṃ tu yad vācyaṃ tasya cet pratipādane savyāpārā guṇās tatra sarvasyoktiḥ sakṛcchrutau  BVaky prakārādhārabhedena viśeṣe samavasthitaḥ śabdāntarābhisaṃbandhe sāmānyavacanaḥ katham  BVaky sādṛśyamātraṃ sāmānyaṃ dviṣṭhaṃ kaiś cit pratīyate guṇo bhede py abhedena dvivṛttir vā vivakṣitaḥ  BVaky vyāpāro jātibhāgasya dravyayor vābhidhitsitaḥ rūpāt sāmānyavācitvaṃ prāg vā vṛtter udāhṛtam  BVaky vyāghraśabdo yadā śauryāt puruṣārthe vatiṣṭhate tadādhikaraṇābhedāt samāsasyāsti saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky śūraśabdaprayoge tu vyāghraśabdo mṛge sthitaḥ bhinne dhikaraṇe vṛttes tatra naivāsti saṃbhavaḥ  BVaky sāmānādhikaraṇye pi guṇabhedasya saṃbhavāt prayogaḥ śūraśabdasya samāse py anuṣajyate  BVaky pūjopādhiś ca yo dṛṣṭaḥ kutsanopādhayaś ca ye teṣāṃ bhinnanimittatvān niyamārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ  BVaky asaṃbhave pi vā vṛtteḥ syād etal liṅgadarśanam acver iti yathā liṅgam abhāve pi bhṛśādiṣu  BVaky vatyantāvayave vākye yad aupamyaṃ pratīyate tatpratyayavidhau sūtre nirdeśo yaṃ vicāryate  BVaky kriyety upādhiḥ prāthamyāt prakṛtyarthasya yady api na prātipadikaṃ tatra kriyāvācy upapadyate  BVaky sattvavṛttasya śeṣe vā tṛtīyā sādhane pi vā tiṅām asattvavācitvād ubhayaṃ tan na vidyate  BVaky pākādayas tṛtīyāntāḥ sattvadharmasamanvayāt na kriyety apadiśyante kṛtvo rthapratyaye yathā  BVaky ye cāvyayakṛtaḥ ke cit kriyādharmasamanvitāḥ teṣām asattvavācitvaṃ tiṅantair na viśiṣyate  BVaky kṛtvasujviṣayā yāpi śayitavyādiṣu kriyā upamānopameyatvaṃ tatrātyantam asaṃbhavi  BVaky na kevalau dravyaguṇau tadvān vāpy upamīyate śayitavyādibhis teṣu nopamārtho sti kaś cana  BVaky upamānopameyatve dravye cānuktadharmiṇi nimittatvena gamyante rūḍhayogāḥ kriyāguṇāḥ  BVaky hotavyasadṛśo hotety atrāpy artho na vidyate virodhāt kriyayā tasmāt kriyāvān nopamīyate  BVaky kriyā samānajātiyā tadbhāvān nopamīyate jātibhede pi pākena bhinnāḥ pākādayaḥ kriyāḥ  BVaky ādhārabhedād bhinnāyām upamānasya saṃbhavaḥ adhyetavyena viprāṇāṃ tulyam adhyayanaṃ viśām  BVaky arthāt prakaraṇād vāpi yatrāpekṣyaṃ pratīyate sāmarthyād anapekṣasya tasya vṛttiḥ prasajyate  BVaky tailapākena tulye ca ghṛtapāke vivakṣite kriyāvad api kāryāṇāṃ darśanāt pratyayo bhavet  BVaky atiṅgrahaṇam evaṃ tu samāsasya nivartakam gamanaṃ kārakasyeti ṇvuly anyasmin na saṃbhavet  BVaky sarvasya parihārārthaṃ samudāyatvam āśritam śuddhāyāḥ saṃbhavān na syāt kriyāyā brāhmaṇādiṣu  BVaky upamānavivakṣāyāṃ svadharmaś ca nivartate kriyāyā na śrutād yasmād upamānaṃ samāpyate  BVaky tṛtīyo py āśrito bhedo dharmaḥ sādhāraṇo dvayoḥ vyāpāravān na kṛtsnasya sāmyaṃ kṛtsnena vidyate  BVaky dravye vāpi kriyāyāṃ vā nimittāt tat prakalpate kriyāṇāṃ vidyamānatvād vṛttir na syād gavādiṣu  BVaky abhāvāt kevalāyās tu tadvān arthaḥ pratīyate pradhānāsaṃbhave yuktā lakṣaṇārthā kriyāśrutiḥ  BVaky kriyāntareṣu sāpekṣāḥ kriyāśabdāḥ kriyāntare upakārāya gṛhyante yathaiva brāhmaṇādayaḥ  BVaky yathā prakarṣaḥ sarvatra nimittāntarahetukaḥ dravyavad guṇaśabde pi sa nimittam apekṣate  BVaky yo ya uccāryate śabdaḥ sa svarūpanibandhanaḥ yathā tathopamāneṣu vyapekṣa na nivartate  BVaky kriyāvṛttes tṛtīyāntasy aivaṃ cāsaṃbhave sati prasiddhanyāyakaraṇo bhāṣye yujir udāhṛtaḥ  BVaky antarbhūte tu karaṇe prayogo na punar bhavet nyāyenāyuktam ity atra jīvatau prāṇakarmavat  BVaky śāstrābhyāsāc ca bhedo yam ayuktam iti varṇyate aśobhanam asaṃbaddham iti rūḍhir vyavasthitā  BVaky vivibhaktiḥ prakṛtyarthaṃ praty upādhiḥ kathaṃ bhavet vibhaktipariṇāme ca prakalpyaṃ viṣayāntaram  BVaky vibhaktyantarayogo hi yasya tad viṣayāntare vibhaktyantarasaṃbandhaḥ sāmarthyād anumīyate  BVaky sārūpyāt tu tad evedam iti tatropacaryate śabdāntaraṃ vibhaktyā tu yuktaṃ śāstre tad aśrutam  BVaky prakṛtiś cet tṛtīyāntā tenety asmāt pratīyate kriyeti prathamāntā sā kathaṃ bhavitum arhati  BVaky kriyayeti tṛtīyā ca prayoge kasya kalpyatām tenety asya hi saṃbandhaḥ sūtrasthena na vidyate  BVaky sopaskāreṣu sūtreṣu vākyaśeṣaḥ samarthyate tena yat tat tṛtīyāntaṃ kriyā cet seti gamyate  BVaky upādheḥ kasya cid vākye prayoga upalabhyate pratīyamānadharmānyo na kadā cit prayujyate  BVaky nīlam utpalam ity atra na viśeṣye na bhedake kaś cit taddharmavacano vākye śabdaḥ prayujyate  BVaky atyantānugamāt tatra na sūtre na ca vigrahe vibhaktipariṇāmena kiṃ cid asti prayojanam  BVaky tṛtīyāntaṃ kriyety etad vigrahe na prayujyate yathā daṇḍaḥ praharaṇaṃ krīḍāyām iti dṛśyate  BVaky ghavidhau yac ca saṃjñāyām iti sūtra udāhṛtam upādānaṃ prayogeṣu tasyātyantaṃ na vidyate  BVaky yair aprayuktaiḥ saṃskāraḥ pradhāneṣu pratīyate te bhede pi vibhaktīnāṃ nirdiśyanta upādhayaḥ  BVaky samudāyeṣu vartante bhāvānāṃ sahacāriṇām śabdās tat tv avivakṣāyāṃ samuccayavikalpayoḥ  BVaky samuccayas tu kriyate yeṣu pratyarthavṛttiṣu bhedādhiṣṭhānayā yogas tesāṃ bhavati saṃkhyayā  BVaky sarvair viśiṣṭās tair arthair janyante sahacāribhiḥ buddhayaḥ pratipattṝṇāṃ śabdārthāṃs tān ato viduḥ  BVaky saṃsṛṣṭāḥ pratyayeṣv arthāḥ sarva evopakārinaḥ teṣāṃ pratyayarūpeṇa sarveṣāṃ śabdavācyatā  BVaky kevalānāṃ tu bhāvānāṃ na rūpam avadhāryate anirūpitarūpeṣu teṣu śabdo na vartate  BVaky pūrvaśabdaprayogāc ca samūhān na nivartate vartate vayave nāpi nopāttaṃ tyajate kva cit  BVaky samudāyābhidhāyi ca yadi bhedaṃ viśeṣayet tatrātulyavibhaktitvaṃ pūrvakāyādivad bhavet  BVaky samūhe ca pradeśe ca pañcālā iti dṛśyate tathā viśeṣaṇaṃ sarva ity etad upapadyate  BVaky tathārdhapippalīty atra jātyantaranivṛttaye ardhaṃ ca pippalī ceti khande śabdaḥ pratīyate  BVaky pañcālānāṃ pradeśo pi bhinno janapadāntarāt tatrānyasya nivṛttyarthe śabde bhedo na gamyate  BVaky prasiddhās tu viśeṣeṇa samudāye vyavasthitāḥ pradeśe darśanaṃ teṣām arthaprakaraṇādibhiḥ  BVaky yad upavyañjanaṃ jāteḥ sahacāri ca karmasu tatra vā rūḍhasaṃbandhaṃ yat prāyeṇopalakṣitam  BVaky samudāyaḥ pradeśo vety evaṃ tasminn anāśrite arthātmany aviśeṣeṇa vartante brāhmaṇādayaḥ  BVaky yaś ca tulyaśrutir dṛṣṭaḥ samudāye vyavasthitaḥ tenopacaritaikatvaṃ pradeśe py upalabhyate  BVaky saṃskārād upaghātād vā vṛtto ktaparimāṇake tailādau jātiśabdo tra sāmarthyād avasīyate  BVaky na jātiguṇaśabdeṣu mūrtibhedo vivakṣitaḥ te jātiguṇasaṃbandha bhedamātranibandhanāḥ  BVaky kṛṣṇādivyapadeśaś ca sarvāvayavavṛttibhiḥ guṇais te py ekadeśasthāḥ paṭādīnāṃ viśeṣakāḥ  BVaky paṭāvayavavṛttās tu yadā tatra paṭādayaḥ tadā tailādivat teṣāṃ jātiśabdatvam ucyate  BVaky nivṛttyarthā śrutir yeṣāṃ bhedas teṣv anapekṣitaḥ pradeśe samudāye vā guṇo nyeṣāṃ nivartakaḥ  BVaky brāhmaṇādhyayane tatra vartate brāhmaṇaśrutiḥ sādṛśyaṃ tatra dṛṣṭaṃ hi kṣatriyādhyayanādibhiḥ  BVaky brāhmaṇādhyayane vṛttir yadi syād brāhmaṇaśruteḥ vaktavyaṃ kena dharmeṇa tulyatvaṃ kriyayor iti  BVaky adhyetari yadā vṛttir ucyate brāhmaṇaśruteḥ nimittatvaṃ tadopaiti kriyaivādhyetari sthitā  BVaky simhaśabdena saṃbandhe gauryamātrābhidhāyinā caitrāt ṣaṣṭhī prasajyeta yoge śattryādibhir yathā  BVaky brāhmaṇāyeva dātavyaṃ vaiśyāyety evamādiṣu saṃpradānādiyogaś ca kriyāmātre na kalpate  BVaky kriyāmātrābhidhāyitvād avyayeṣu vater na ca pāṭhaḥ kadā cit kartavyas tulyau pakṣāv ubhau yataḥ  BVaky jahāti jātiṃ dravyaṃ vā tasmān nāvayave sthitaḥ kriyāyās tu śrutir yasmāt tadvaty arthe vatiṣṭhate  BVaky akriyāṇāṃ nivṛttyarthāyataś cātra kriyāśrutiḥ kriyopalakṣite tasmāt kriyāśabdaḥ pratīyate  BVaky hotavyādiṣu yasmāc ca kriyānyā brāhmaṇādivat apekṣaṇīyā śuddhe rthe tasmād vṛttir na kasya cit  BVaky sarvaṃ vāpy ekadeśo vā yasminn āśriyate kva cit viśeṣavṛttiṃ taṃ sarvam āhur bhede vyavasthitam  BVaky samuccayo vikalpo vā prakārāḥ sarva eva vā viśeṣā iti varṇyante sāmānyaṃ vāvikalpitam  BVaky na hi brāhmaṇa ity atra bhedaḥ kaś cid apāśritaḥ apākṛto vā tenāyaṃ samudāye vyavasthitaḥ  BVaky kriyā tv āśrīyate yasmin sa bhedo dhyavasīyate tathānyathā sarvathā cety aprayoge na vidyate  BVaky upamāne kriyāvṛttim upameye kriyāśrutiḥ pratyāyayantī bhedasya karotīva padārthatām  BVaky vyāpāreṇaiva sādṛśye vyāpārasya vivakṣite kriyāvadvacanāc chabdāt pratyayaḥ pratipādyate  BVaky kriyāvato pi sādṛśye vaktum iṣṭe kriyāvatā adhyetā brāhmaṇa iva pratyayo na nivartate  BVaky adhīte tulya ity evaṃ puṃlliṅgena viśeṣaṇam kriyāvati kriyāyāṃ tu tulyaśabde napuṃsakam  BVaky prakṛtyarthe viśiṣṭe pi pratyayārthāviśeṣaṇāt putreṇa tulyaḥ kapila iti vṛttiḥ prasajyate  BVaky yāḥ putre rūḍhasaṃbandhāḥ kriyā loke vivakṣitāḥ tābhiḥ kriyāvataḥ putrād guṇatulye vatir bhavet  BVaky antarbhūtaṃ nimittaṃ ca rūḍhiśabdeṣu yady api kriyās tu sahacāriṇyo rūḍhāḥ santi padārthavat  BVaky kramaṃ tu yadi bādhitvā pratyayārthaviśeṣaṇam pradhānānugrahāt sāmyād vibhakteś cāvatiṣṭhate  BVaky prakṛter aviśiṣṭatvāt kriyātulye prasajyate putrādau guṇaśabdebhyaḥ pūrvoktasya viparyaye  BVaky sthūlena tulyo yātīti bahiraṅgā kriyāśrutiḥ animittaṃ vates tulyaṃ yātīty atreṣyate vatiḥ  BVaky dvayaṃ viśeṣyate tena yad ekatra viśeṣaṇaṃ tulyaśabdo hi taṃ dharmam ubhayastham apekṣate  BVaky ekaḥ samāno dharmaś ced upamānopameyayoḥ tulayā saṃmitaṃ tulyam iti tatropapadyate  BVaky sūtre śrutaś ca dviṣṭho sāv abhedena pratīyate na ca sāmānyaśabdatvād aśrutā gamyate kriyā  BVaky aśrutāś ca pratīyante nideśasthāyitādayaḥ ye dharmā niyatās teṣāṃ putrādiṣu na vidyate  BVaky anāśritakriyas tasmān na tulyo sti kriyāvatā kriyāyāḥ śravaṇe sāpi kriyāvattā pratīyate  BVaky dvayoḥ pratividhānāc ca jyāyastvam abhidhīyate nityāsattvābhidhāyitvāt pratyayārthaviśeṣaṇe  BVaky asattvabhūto vyāpāraḥ kevalaḥ pratyaye yataḥ vidyate lakṣaṇārthatvaṃ nāsti tena kriyāśruteḥ  BVaky kriyāvatas tu grahaṇāt prakṛtyarthaviśeṣaṇe kriyāmātrena tulyatve siddhāsattvābhidhāyitā  BVaky yadā kriyānimittaṃ tu sādṛśyaṃ syāt kriyāvatoḥ kriyāvato bhidheyatvāt tadā dravyābhidhāyitā  BVaky avyayeṣu vateḥ pāṭhaḥ kāryas tatra svarādivat brāhmaṇena samo dhyetety atra ca pratyayo bhavet  BVaky sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca vatyarthenāpadiśyate tulyam ity anyathā kalpyo vākyaśeṣo śruto bhavet  BVaky kriyāvatoś ca sādṛśye pratyayārthaviśeṣaṇe adhyetrā sadṛśo dhyetety atra nāsti vater vidhiḥ  BVaky tulyārthair iti yā tasyās tṛtīyāyā na bhidyate artho bhede pi sarvābhir itarābhir vibhaktibhiḥ  BVaky bhojyate brāhmaṇa iva tulyaṃ bhuktaṃ dvijātinā paśyati brāhmaṇam iva tulyaṃ vipreṇa paśyati  BVaky brāhmaṇeneva vijñātaṃ tulyaṃ jñātaṃ dvijātinā dīyatāṃ brāhmaṇāyeva tulyaṃ vipreṇa dīyatām  BVaky brāhmaṇād iva vaiśyāt tvam adhīṣvādhyayanaṃ bahu ity evamādibhir bhedas tṛtīyāyā na kaś cana  BVaky tulyaṃ madhurayādhīye mātrā tulyaṃ smarāmi tām madhurāyāś ca mātuś ca kathaṃ sādṛśyakalpanā  BVaky madhurāviṣayaḥ pāṭhaḥ smaraṇaṃ mātṛkarmakam madhurāmātṛśabdābhyām abhedenābhidhīyate  BVaky uṣṭrāvayavatulyeṣu mukheṣūṣṭraśrutir yathā vartate gṛhatulye ca prāsāde madhurāśrutiḥ  BVaky yathādhyayanayoḥ sāmyam adhyetror apadiśyate tathā kriyāgatair dharmair ucyante sādhanāśrayāḥ  BVaky ivārthe yac ca vacanaṃ pūrvasūtre ca yo vidhiḥ kriyāśabdaśrutau bhedo na kaś cid vidyate tayoḥ  BVaky yady apy upādhir anyatra niyato na prayujyate rūpābhedāt tv anirjñātā kriyātra śrūyate punaḥ  BVaky yathā vyutparayaḥ pucchau kyaṅante sudurādayaḥ saty api pratyayārthatve bhedābhāvād udāhṛtāḥ  BVaky evaṃ ca sati pūrveṇa siddho trāpi vater vidhiḥ niyame vābhidhāne vā bhidyate na kriyāśrutiḥ  BVaky ive dravyādiviṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ punar ucyate kriyāṇām eva sadṛśve pūrvasūtre vidhīyate  BVaky madhurāyām iva gṛhā brāhmaṇasyeva pāṇḍurāḥ ity atra dravyaguṇayoḥ pūrveṇa na vatir bhavet  BVaky ārambhasyākriyārthatve nārtho yogena vidyate ṛte kriyāyā grahaṇāt pūrvayogena sidhyati  BVaky madhurāvayave vṛttir vvākhyātā madhurāśruteḥ brāhmaṇāvayavān dantān vakṣyati brāhmaṇaśrutiḥ  BVaky na kā cid ivayoge tu bāhyāt saṃbandhino ṣaṣṭhī vidhīyate tatra pūrveṇa pratyayo bhavet  BVaky ādhikyaṃ tulyaśabdena saṃbandha upajāyate ṣaṣṭhītṛtīye tatra stas tulyaśabdo hi vācakaḥ  BVaky ivaśabdaprayoge tu bāhyāt saṃbandhino vinā nādhikyam upamāne sti dyotakaḥ sa prayujyate  BVaky ive yo vyatireko tra sa prāsādādihetukaḥ tulye tadviṣayāpekṣam ādhikyam upajāyate  BVaky gavayena samo nadvān iti vṛttis tathā bhavet na tv asti gaur ivety atra vyatireka ivāśrayaḥ  BVaky upameyena saṃbandhāt prāk prāsādādihetuke vyatireke vater bhāvo na tulyārthatvahetuke  BVaky ivaśabdena saṃbandhe na tṛtīyā vidhīyate prakṛtāṃ tām atas tyaktvā vibhaktyantaraṃ āśritam  BVaky saptamy api na tatrāsti jñāpakārthā tu sā kṛtā iṣṭā sā śeṣaviṣaye niyatāsu vibhaktiṣu  BVaky yadi tu vyatirekeṇa viṣaye smin vibhaktayaḥ pravarteraṃs tṛtīyaiva vyabhicāraṃ pradarśayet  BVaky vyabhicāre tathā siddhe saptamīgrahaṇād vinā saptamy evocyate sarvā na santy anyā vibhaktayaḥ  BVaky atyantam atra viṣaye saptamyā jñāpakārthayā bādhitā vinivarteta ṣaṣṭhī sā gṛhyate punaḥ  BVaky pūrvābhyām eva yogābhyāṃ vigrahāntarakalpanāt arhārthe pi vatiḥ siddhaḥ sa tv ekena nidarśyate  BVaky tena tulyam iti prāpte kriyopādhiḥ prasidhyati rājavad vartate rājety atra bhede vivakṣite  BVaky rājatvena prasiddhā ye pṛthuprabhṛtayo nṛpāḥ yudhiṣṭhirāntās te nyeṣām upamānaṃ mahīkṣitām  BVaky siddhyasiddhikṛto bheda upamānopameyayoḥ sarvatraiva yato siddhaṃ prasiddhenopamīyate  BVaky rājavad rūpam asyeti rājany eva vivakṣite akriyārthena yogena dvitīyena bhaviṣyati  BVaky upamānāvivakṣāyāṃ niyamārtho yam ucyate dharmo rhatikriyākartā tadarthaṃ vacanaṃ punaḥ  BVaky kṛtahastavad ity etat prasiddheṣv eva dṛśyate rājatvena prasiddhe ca rājñi rājavad ity api  BVaky arājñi yeṣāṃ dharmāṇāṃ dṛṣṭo tyantam asaṃbhavaḥ te rājani niyamyante tyajyante vyabhicāriṇaḥ  BVaky arhateś ca kriyā kartrī yā tasyāṃ vatir iṣyate rājānam arhati cchattram iti na tv evamādiṣu  BVaky prayuktānāṃ hi śabdānāṃ śāstreṇānugamaḥ satām chattrādyarthe tu vacane pratyākhyānaṃ na saṃbhavet  BVaky tadarham iti nārabdhaṃ sūtraṃ vyākaraṇāntare saṃbhavaty upamātrāpi bhedasya parikalpanāt  BVaky ekasya kāryanirjñānāt siddhasya viṣayāntare taddharmatvavivakṣāyāṃ buddhyā bhedaḥ prakalpyate  BVaky sūtrārambhān na caitasmād ivaśabdasya vidyate prayogaḥ so pi caitasya viṣaye vidyate vateḥ  BVaky dasyuhendra ivety etad aindramantre prayujyate anyatra dṛṣṭakarmendro yathety asmin vivakṣite  BVaky pūrvām avasthām āśritya yāvasthā vyapadiśyate sadṛśas tvaṃ tavaiveti tatraivam abhidhīyate  BVaky prasiddhabhedaṃ yatrānyad upamānaṃ na vidyate upameyasya tatrātmā svabuddhyā pravibhajyate  BVaky yo pi svābhāviko bhedaḥ so pi buddhinibandhanaḥ tenāsmin viṣaye bhinnam abhinnaṃ vā na vidyate  BVaky aṅgadī kuṇḍalī ceti darśayan bhedahetubhiḥ caitram īdṛśam ity āha buddhyavasthāparigrahāt  BVaky etaiḥ śabdair yathābhūtaḥ pratyayātmopajāyate tatpratyayānukāreṇa viṣayo py upapadyate  BVaky buddhyavasthāvibhāgena bhedakāryaṃ pratīyate janyanta iva śabdānām arthāḥ sarve vivakṣayā  BVaky tathāvidhe pi bāhye rthe bhidyante yatra buddhayaḥ na tatra kaś cit sādṛśyaṃ sad api pratipadyate  BVaky atyantaṃ viṣaye bhinne yāvat prakhyā na bhidyate na tāvat pratyabhijñānaṃ kasya cid vinivartate  BVaky ayam eva tu sūtreṇa bhedo bhedena darśitaḥ prasiddham api durjñānam abudhaḥ pratipadyate  BVaky vaiyākaraṇavad brūte na vaiyākaraṇaḥ sadā vaiyākaraṇavad brūṣvety ataḥ so py abhidhīyate  BVaky ke cit pumāṃso bhāṣante strīvat puṃvac ca yoṣitaḥ vyabhicāre svadharmo pi punas tenopadiśyate  BVaky sadṛśas tvaṃ tavaiveti loke yad abhidhīyate upamānāntaraṃ tatra prasaktaṃ vinivartate  BVaky yuktam aupayikaṃ rājña ity arthasya nidarśane upamānāvivakṣāyāṃ tadarham iti paṭhyate  BVaky prasaktānuprasaktas tu vatiśeṣo bhidhīyate upamānābhisaṃbandhād asmin vatir udāhṛtaḥ  BVaky pradhānakalpanābhāve guṇaśabdasya darśanāt upasargād vatau siddhā dhātau dhātvarthakalpanā  BVaky svaṃ rūpam iti caitasminn arthasyāpi parigrahaḥ rūpavaj jñāpitas tasmād āsanno rtho grahīṣyate  BVaky dhātvarthenopajanitaṃ sādhanatvena sādhanam dhātunā kṛtam ity evam asmin sūtre pratīyate  BVaky yaḥ śabdaś caritārthatvād atyantaṃ na prayujyate viṣaye darśanāt tatra lopas tasyābhidhīyate  BVaky kriyāyāṃ sādhane dravye prādayo ye vyavasthitāḥ tebhyaḥ sattvābhidhāyibhyo vatiḥ svārthe vidhīyate  BVaky pratyayena vinā prādis tatrārthe na prayujyate bhedena tu samākhyāne vibhāgaḥ parikalpitaḥ  BVaky anaṅgīkṛtasattvaṃ tu yadi gṛhyeta sādhanam vibhaktibhir niyogaḥ syād yathaiva tasilādiṣu  BVaky pāṭhād yair avibhaktitvaṃ vatyanteṣv anugamyate teṣām udvata ity atra vaktavyā savibhaktitā  BVaky vatyarthaṃ nāvagāhete puṃvad ity asya darśanāt nañsnañāv apavādasya bādhakaṃ tan nipātanam  BVaky etam utkrāmato nūnaṃ vatyarthaṃ nañsnañāv iti tayoḥ pravṛttāv utsargo bādhanān nopapadyate  BVaky nañsnañau vihitau yena sa yogo nāvagāhate vatiprakaraṇaṃ tad dhi liṅgam evaṃ samarthyate  BVaky abhedenopamānasya bhinnārthopanipātitā ūhas tathopamānānām aṅgavan nopalabhyate  BVaky gāvedhuke carau dṛṣṭā govikartākṣavāpayoḥ paśū rudra iva hy etāv ity ekavacanaśrutiḥ  BVaky upamānasya bhedāc ca bahuṣu syād año vidhiḥ kāśyapā iti lopaḥ syāt tathā pratikṛtiṣv api  BVaky evaṃ tu yuktavadbhāvād atraikavacanaṃ bhavet lum manuṣye tathoktaṃ syāl liṅgasyaikasya siddhaye  BVaky upameyeṣu bhinneṣu kiṃ cid ekaṃ pravartate pratyayasya vidhau tatra nityaṃ yuktavad iṣyate  BVaky yadā pratyupameyaṃ tu tad ekaikam avasthitam tadā bāhyārthabhedena taddhitāntaṃ pracīyate  BVaky yathā samūhapracaye dvigūnāṃ bhinnasaṃkhyatā pañcapūlyādiṣu tathā lubantapracayo bhavet  BVaky pracaye bhidyamāne tu saṃkhyā pūleṣu bhidyate arthabhedo lubanteṣu naivaṃ kaś cana dṛśyate  BVaky yeṣūpameyavacanaḥ śabdo nyo na prayujyate upamānasya tatrānyaiḥ saṃkhyāyā bheda iṣyate  BVaky yathā guḍatilādīnāṃ prayogād ekasaṃkhyatā pākāder aprayoge tu bhinnā saṃkhyābhidhīyate  BVaky yaḥ saṃbandhigato bhedaḥ sa prayoge pratīyate saṃbandhinām ato bheda upameye na gamyate  BVaky tasmāt sāmānyaśabdatva prasaṅgavinivṛttaye upameyagato bheda upamāneṣu dṛśyate  BVaky upamānaṃ samastānām abhinnam śrūyate kva cit bhinnānām upameyanām ekaikam vopamīyate  BVaky yathā garuḍa ity etad vyūhāpekṣaṃ prayujyate ekena yatra sādṛśyaṃ vainateyena hastinām  BVaky ekasyāpi pratīyeta bhinnā pratikṛtiḥ saha kāśyapasyeti tenāyaṃ pratyekam avatiṣṭhate  BVaky meghāḥ śaila ivety ukte samastānāṃ pratīyate sādṛśyam giriṇaikena pratyekaṃ tena bhidyate  BVaky chāpekṣā tadviṣayatā vidheyatvān na gamyate kākatālīyam ity atra prasiddham hy upalakṣaṇam  BVaky rājāśvādiś ca viṣayaḥ syād anyo vety aniścitam tena cchasya vidhānāt prāg vyapadeśo na vidyate  BVaky dvayor ivārthayor atra nimittatvaṃ pratīyate ekenāvayavo yuktaḥ pratyayo nyena yujyate  BVaky caitrasya tatrāgamanaṃ kākasyāgamanaṃ yathā dasyor abhinipātas tu tālasya patanaṃ yathā  BVaky saṃnipāte tayor yānyā kriyā tatropajāyate vadhādir upameye rthe tayā chavidhir iṣyate  BVaky kriyāyāṃ samavetāyāṃ dravyaśabdo vatiṣṭhate pātāgamanayoḥ kāka tālaśabdau tathā sthitau  BVaky yad anvākhyāyakaṃ vākyaṃ tad evaṃ parikalpyate prayogavākvaṃ yal loke tad evaṃ na prayujyate  BVaky yayor atarkitā prāptir dṛśyate kākatālavat tayoḥ samāsaprakṛter vṛttir abhyupagamyate  BVaky kākasya tālena yathā vadho yasya tu dasyunā tatra citrīkṛte nyasminn upameye cha iṣyate  BVaky cañcatprakāraś cañcatko bṛhatka iti cāpare maṇimaḍḍūkakhadyotān sādṛśvena pracakṣate  BVaky tatronmeṣanimeṣābhyāṃ khadyota upamīyate śvāsaprabandhair maṇḍūkaḥ spandamānaprabho maṇiḥ  BVaky pravikāsiprabho lpo pi mahān ya upalabhyate bṛhatka iti tatraiṣa maṇau śabdaḥ prayujyate  BVaky sādṛśyam eva sarvatra prakāraḥ kaiś cid iṣyate bhede pi tu prakārākhyā kaiś cid abhyupagamyate  BVaky prakāravacanaḥ kaś cit prakāravati saṃsthitaḥ prakāramātre vartitvā kaś cit tadvati vartate  BVaky sādṛśyagrahaṇaṃ sūtre sadṛśasyopalakṣaṇam tulyayor avyayībhāve sahaśabdo bhidhāyakaḥ  BVaky vipsāsādṛśyayor vṛttir yā yathārthābhidhāyinaḥ sa cāyam avyayībhāve bhedo bhedena darśitaḥ  BVaky sādṛśyaṃ yogyatā kaiś cid anāv abhyupagamyate yat tu mūrtigataṃ sāmyaṃ tat sahenābhidhīyate  BVaky itthaṃbhāve pi sādṛśyaṃ buddhyavasthānibandhanam grahaṇe bhedamātrasya tatrānyaivābhidhīyate  BVaky gaur vāhīka iti dvitve sādṛśyaṃ pratyudāhṛtam śuklādau sati niṣpanne vāhīko na dvir ucyate  BVaky iti bhartṛharikṛtaṃ vākyapadīyam samāptam
